﻿                                                       Parties                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
This Exploration and Production Concession Contract (“EPC”) is made subject to         <br /><br /><br />
applicable law on the........day of December 2006:                                     <br /><br /><br />
(a)    THE GOVERNMENT OF THE REPUBLIC OF MOZAMBIQUE, hereinafter                       <br /><br /><br />
referred to as “the Government” and herein represented by the Minister for Mineral     <br /><br /><br />
Resources; and                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
(b)    ENI EAST AFRICA S.p.A., a company established under the laws of Italy           <br /><br /><br />
hereinafter referred to as “Eni” and herein represented by the appointed               <br /><br /><br />
representative, and                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(c)    EMPRESA NACIONAL DE HIDROCARBONETOS, E.P., a company established                <br /><br /><br />
in accordance with the laws of the Republic of Mozambique, herein represented by       <br /><br /><br />
its Chairman of the Board hereinafter referred to as “ENH”.                            <br /><br /><br />
Eni and ENH shall hereinafter be referred to as the “Concessionaire”. The              <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire and the Government shall hereinafter collectively be referred to as     <br /><br /><br />
the “Parties”.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />

﻿ Preamble                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
WHEREAS, applicable Petroleum law provides that all Petroleum resources in the soil and           <br /><br /><br />
the subsoil of the land territory, in the seabed of internal waters and the territorial sea, in   <br /><br /><br />
the exclusive economic zone and on the continental shelf, are the property of the Republic        <br /><br /><br />
of Mozambique;                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
WHEREAS, pursuant to applicable Petroleum law, the Government has the authority to                <br /><br /><br />
ensure the implementation of the policy for Petroleum Operations and has for the purpose          <br /><br /><br />
of this EPC appointed the Ministry of Mineral Resources, hereinafter referred to as               <br /><br /><br />
“MIREM”, to carry out certain functions for and on behalf of the Government as hereafter          <br /><br /><br />
specified;                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
WHEREAS, the Government desires to award to Eni and ENH the right to undertake                    <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Exploration, Development and Production in certain areas subject to the                 <br /><br /><br />
jurisdiction of the Republic of Mozambique;                                                       <br /><br /><br />
WHEREAS, the Concessionaire is willing, on certain terms and conditions stipulated to             <br /><br /><br />
undertake Petroleum Exploration, Development and Production in the EPC Area and has               <br /><br /><br />
for such purpose technical competence and adequate financial resources;                           <br /><br /><br />
WHEREAS, the applicable Petroleum law provides that Petroleum Exploration,                        <br /><br /><br />
Development and Production shall be carried out under a concession;                               <br /><br /><br />
NOW THEREFORE it has been concluded as follows:                                                   <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                         Article 1                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                       EPC Documents                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
The EPC consists of this EPC main document and the following Annexes, which form an                <br /><br /><br />
integral part hereof:                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 Annex “A”                            Description of the EPC Area                                  <br /><br /><br />
 Annex “B”                            Map of the EPC Area                                          <br /><br /><br />
 Annex “C”                            Accounting and Financial Procedure                           <br /><br /><br />
 Annex “D”                            Form of Bank Guarantee                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 Annex “E”                            Form of Parent Company Guarantee                             <br /><br /><br />
 Annex “F”                            Joint Operating Agreement                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
Subject to the conclusion of the EPC, the Concessionaire shall submit a signed joint               <br /><br /><br />
operating agreement as stipulated in Annex F, for which Government approval is a                   <br /><br /><br />
condition under this EPC.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
In the event of conflict between the provisions of the EPC main document and its Annexes,          <br /><br /><br />
the EPC main document shall prevail.                                                               <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                         Article 2                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                        Definitions                                             <br /><br /><br />
Definitions stipulated in applicable Mozambican Petroleum law, currently Law no. 3/2001         <br /><br /><br />
of 21 February and Decree No. 24/2004 of 20 August apply to this EPC unless otherwise           <br /><br /><br />
expressly defined . Words and phrases used in this EPC including its Annexes shall have         <br /><br /><br />
the following meanings:                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
“Affiliated Company" means, in relation to any Person constituting the Concessionaire,          <br /><br /><br />
any parent company which directly or indirectly controls such Person or any company             <br /><br /><br />
which is directly controlled by such Person or any company which is controlled, directly or     <br /><br /><br />
indirectly, by any such parent company.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
For the purpose of the foregoing definition:                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(a)    a company is directly controlled by another company or companies holding shares or       <br /><br /><br />
other equity ownership carrying in the aggregate more than fifty percent (50%) of the           <br /><br /><br />
voting rights exercisable at general meetings; and                                              <br /><br /><br />
(b)    a particular company is indirectly controlled by a company or companies (“parent         <br /><br /><br />
company or companies”) if a series of companies can be specified, beginning with                <br /><br /><br />
the parent company or companies and ending with the particular company, so related              <br /><br /><br />
that each company of the series, except the parent company or companies, is directly            <br /><br /><br />
controlled by one or more of the companies earlier in the series.                               <br /><br /><br />
“Commercial Assessment Period" applies to a Discovery Area and means the period                 <br /><br /><br />
commencing at the time when the appraisal report regarding the Appraisal Programme              <br /><br /><br />
relating to the Discovery of non-Associated Natural Gas has been submitted by the               <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
“Commercial Production ” means production of Petroleum and delivery of the same at the          <br /><br /><br />
Delivery Point under a programme of production and sale as provided for in a                    <br /><br /><br />
Development Plan as amended from time to time.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
        “Cost Petroleum ” means the portion of Petroleum Produced available to the              <br /><br /><br />
  Concessionaires to cover the costs and expenses incurred in carrying out the Petroleum        <br /><br /><br />
 Km'ution copy                                         4                                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿Operations as stipulated in the EPC.                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
“Decommissioning Fund” means the fund established to cover the costs of                         <br /><br /><br />
decommissioning operations.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
“Delivery Point” means the point in the Republic of Mozambique which, in the case of            <br /><br /><br />
Natural Gas, is the inlet flange of the transmission pipeline, and in the case of Crude Oil     <br /><br /><br />
the inlet flange of the lifting tankship or, in either case, such other point as may be agreed  <br /><br /><br />
by MIREM and the Concessionaire.                                                                <br /><br /><br />
“Effective Date” means the first day of the month following the date on which this EPC          <br /><br /><br />
has been signed by the Government and the Concessionaire, the conditions in Article 3.2         <br /><br /><br />
have been met, and the ruling of the Administrative Tribunal has been obtained.                 <br /><br /><br />
“Evaluation Period” means the period, following a notice by the Concessionaire that it has      <br /><br /><br />
made a Discovery, within which the Concessionaire is required to inform MIREM whether           <br /><br /><br />
such Discovery is of potential commercial interest.                                             <br /><br /><br />
“Exclusive Petroleum Operations ” means those Petroleum Operations carried out pursuant         <br /><br /><br />
to applicable law and this EPC chargeable to the account, benefit and liability of less than    <br /><br /><br />
all Persons constituting a Concessionaire under this EPC.                                       <br /><br /><br />
“Expatriate Personnel” means any employee of any Person constituting the                        <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire, of an Affiliated Company of any such Person or of any Subcontractor,            <br /><br /><br />
provided such employee is not a citizen of the Republic of Mozambique and whose                 <br /><br /><br />
contract of employment provides for the payment or the reimbursement of the cost of his         <br /><br /><br />
passage to and from the Republic of Mozambique.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
“Exploration Operations" means operations conducted hereunder for or in connection              <br /><br /><br />
with Exploration for Petroleum in the EPC Area and includes operations conducted to             <br /><br /><br />
carry out an Appraisal Programme or to drill any Appraisal Well.                                <br /><br /><br />
“Exploration Period” means any relevant period of Exploration set out in this EPC.              <br /><br /><br />
“Exploration Well” means any well, the purpose of which at the time of the                      <br /><br /><br />
Execution copy    5                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
﻿commencement of drilling is to explore for an accumulation of Petroleum, which                   <br /><br /><br />
accumulation was at that time unproven by drilling.                                              <br /><br /><br />
“MIREM” means the Ministry of Mineral Resources or any other person or entity                    <br /><br /><br />
appointed to administer and regulate Petroleum Operations for and on behalf of the               <br /><br /><br />
Government under the EPC whose identity has been notified in writing to the                      <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
“Participating Interest" means the percentage interest portion, as further described in          <br /><br /><br />
Article 3.2, of each party constituting the Concessionaire in the rights, privileges, duties     <br /><br /><br />
and obligations derived from this EPC.                                                           <br /><br /><br />
“Person" means any natural person or any corporation, association, partnership, joint            <br /><br /><br />
venture or entity which is considered a legal entity under the law of Mozambique or the          <br /><br /><br />
laws of the country pursuant to which such corporation, association, partnership, joint          <br /><br /><br />
venture or entity is governed.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
“Petroleum Production Tax" means the Imposto sobre a Produgao de Petroleo as defined             <br /><br /><br />
by applicable law.                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
“Petroleum Produced ” means Petroleum which has been extracted from a reservoir,                 <br /><br /><br />
initially separated and processed into Crude Oil, condensate or Natural Gas delivered to the     <br /><br /><br />
Delivery Point appropriate for onwards transportation in bulk or through a pipeline. The         <br /><br /><br />
same applies to “Crude Oil Produced”, “Condensate Produced” and “Natural Gas                     <br /><br /><br />
Produced” as the case may be.                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
“Profit Petroleum" means that portion of Disposable Petroleum, in excess of Cost                 <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum, which is allocated to the Parties under the terms of the EPC.                         <br /><br /><br />
“Subcontractor ” means any Person retained by the Concessionaire to carry out any part of        <br /><br /><br />
the Petroleum Operations.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
"State Participating Interest" means the share of the Participating Interest owned by an         <br /><br /><br />
entity holding this Participating Interest on behalf of the Government.                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 KiccutioB copy                                           6                                      <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                                Article 3                                 <br />
<br><br />
                                                     EPC Rights and their Duration                        <br />
<br><br />
                                                                                                          <br />
<br><br />
3.1 This EPC:                                                                                             <br />
<br><br />
(a)    is a concession awarded pursuant to Petroleum Law (Law No. 3/2001 of 21                            <br />
<br><br />
February), which authorises the conduct of certain Petroleum Exploration,                                 <br />
<br><br />
Development and Production activities in an Area as defined herein;                                       <br />
<br><br />
(b)    confers on the Concessionaire, subject to applicable law and the terms and                         <br />
<br><br />
conditions set forth in this EPC, an exclusive right to conduct Petroleum                                 <br />
<br><br />
Operations in order to produce Petroleum from resources originating from                                  <br />
<br><br />
one or more Petroleum Deposit in the subsoil of the seabed within the limits                              <br />
<br><br />
of the EPC Area;                                                                                          <br />
<br><br />
(c)    save where access to an existing Oil Pipeline or Gas Pipeline System is                            <br />
<br><br />
available on reasonable commercial terms, confers a non- exclusive right                                  <br />
<br><br />
subject to applicable law to construct and operate an Oil Pipeline or Gas                                 <br />
<br><br />
Pipeline System for the purpose of transporting Petroleum Produced from                                   <br />
<br><br />
Petroleum Deposits under this EPC.                                                                        <br />
<br><br />
                                                                                                          <br />
<br><br />
 3.2    (a) Prior to this EPC reaching the Effective Date this EPC has to be approved                     <br />
<br><br />
 by the Council of Ministers, the appurtenant agreements to this EPC have to                              <br />
<br><br />
 be signed by the Concessionaire, and the ruling of the Administrative                                    <br />
<br><br />
 Tribunal has to be obtained.                                                                             <br />
<br><br />
                                                                                                          <br />
<br><br />
                  b) On the Effective Date the respective Participating Interests of Eni is ninety        <br />
<br><br />
                  percent ( 90 %) and of ENH is ten percent (10 %) respectively.                          <br />
<br><br />
                                                                                                          <br />
<br><br />
 3.3 The rights and obligations of the Concessionaire shall commence on the Effective                     <br />
<br><br />
 Date and shall subsist:                                                                                  <br />
<br><br />
 (a)    during the Exploration Period; and                                                                <br />

(d)    to such additional time that may be necessary to give effect to Article 25.4      <br /><br /><br />
on force majeure.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />

the extension;                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

4.1    The Concessionaire shall, in the discharge of its obligations to carry out                                          <br /><br /><br />
Exploration Operations, carry out the work stipulated in this EPC unless otherwise                                         <br /><br /><br />
provided or pay to the Government the sums set forth below in this Article. The                                            <br /><br /><br />
Exploration work commitments stipulated in this Article may not be performed                                               <br /><br /><br />
individually or collectively by the Concessionaire as Exclusive Petroleum                                                  <br /><br /><br />
Operations.                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />

shall conduct the following items collectively referred to as “Exploration work                                            <br /><br /><br />
commitment”:                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
a)    Reprocess and re-interpret of 1000 Km of 2D seismic;                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
b)    Acquire 2000 Km of 2D seismic; and                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
c)    Acquire 1000 SqKm of 3D seismic.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
In case of non-performance of the Exploration work commitment described in this                                            <br /><br /><br />
Article 4.2, save for exemptions listed in this Article, the total amount to be paid by                                    <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire to Government (hereinafter referred to as “Minimum                                                      <br /><br /><br />
Expenditure”) for this period shall be twelve million US dollars (US$ 12,000,000).                                         <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                          a) Drill one (1) Exploration Well to a depth of five thousand meters (5000m)     <br /><br /><br />
                                          from the sea level or to a target of Cretaceous sequences, whichever comes       <br /><br /><br />
                                          first; and                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                          b) Drill one (1) Exploration Well to a depth of five thousand meters (5000m)     <br /><br /><br />

4.5    Should any well forming part of the Exploration work commitment provided for in                                              <br /><br /><br />
Articles 4.3 and 4.4 be abandoned, for any reason other than a reason specified in                                                  <br /><br /><br />
Article 4.6 below, before reaching the defined objectives of such well, the                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire shall drill a substitute well. In this event the relevant Exploration                                                <br /><br /><br />
Period shall be extended by a reasonable period of time as MIREM may agree to                                                       <br /><br /><br />
allow the drilling and evaluation of the substitute well.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
4.6    Unless otherwise approved by MIREM, any well which forms part of the                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Exploration work commitment provided for in Articles 4.3 and 4.4 shall be drilled                                                   <br /><br /><br />
to such depth as set forth in those Articles, unless before reaching the required                                                   <br /><br /><br />
depth:                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />

﻿(a)    further drilling would in the reasonable opinion of the Concessionaire                  <br /><br /><br />
present an obvious danger, due to such events as, but not limited to, the                      <br /><br /><br />
presence of abnormal pressure or excessive losses of drilling mud;                             <br /><br /><br />
(b)    impenetrable formations are encountered;                                                <br /><br /><br />
(c)    Petroleum bearing formations are encountered which require protecting,                  <br /><br /><br />
thereby preventing planned depths from being reached; or                                       <br /><br /><br />
(e) MIREM agrees to terminate the drilling operation.                                          <br /><br /><br />

4.6 it may be terminated at a lesser depth and shall be deemed to have satisfied all           <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire’s obligations in respect of that well.                                      <br /><br /><br />
4.8    During the drilling of Exploration Wells hereunder, the Concessionaire shall, in        <br /><br /><br />

proposed well testing programme;                                                               <br /><br /><br />

Concessionaire and after consultation with MIREM, within the EPC Area                          <br /><br /><br />
indicated by wireline logging or by other means of formation evaluation;                       <br /><br /><br />
and                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(c)    promptly undertake a technical evaluation of the said test results and of all           <br /><br /><br />
other relevant subsurface data and submit the same to MIREM as soon as it                      <br /><br /><br />
has been completed.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />

constituting the Concessionaire has undertaken to fund payments in respect of         <br /><br /><br />
Minimum Expenditure which would otherwise have been payable by another                <br /><br /><br />

that Person constituting the Concessionaire giving that undertaking will be           <br /><br /><br />
deemed to include the share of Minimum Expenditure for which such other               <br /><br /><br />
Person constituting the Concessionaire would have been liable if no such              <br /><br /><br />
undertaking had been given.                                                           <br /><br /><br />

unconditional and irrevocable parent company guarantee from an entity                 <br /><br /><br />
acceptable to MIREM in respect of all its obligations under this EPC beyond the       <br /><br /><br />
scope of the Minimum Expenditure guarantee.                                           <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                           Article 5                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                Conduct of Petroleum Operations                                     <br /><br /><br />
5.1    The Concessionaire shall carry out Petroleum Operations in the EPC Area:                     <br /><br /><br />
(a)    diligently and with due regard to Good Oilfield Practice;                                    <br /><br /><br />
(b)    subject to all applicable laws, specifically the Petroleum Law and the                       <br /><br /><br />
Regulations for Petroleum Operations;                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(c)    in accordance with environmental and safety standards generally accepted                     <br /><br /><br />
in the international petroleum industry and applicable from time to time in                         <br /><br /><br />
similar circumstances;                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(d)    in respect of any Development and Production Area in compliance with the                     <br /><br /><br />
Development Plan for that Development and Production Area.                                          <br /><br /><br />
5.2    Where the Concessionaire is more than one Person any obligation of the                       <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire hereunder shall be a joint and several obligation of the Persons who                 <br /><br /><br />
constitute the Concessionaire, save for the following each of which shall be a                      <br /><br /><br />
several obligation of each of those Persons:                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(a)    the obligation to pay Corporate Income Tax or any other tax assessed and levied on           <br /><br /><br />
profit or net income;                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(b)    the obligation to observe stipulations relating to confidentiality set out in Article 23     <br /><br /><br />
save in respect of their application to anything done or to be done by the Operator                 <br /><br /><br />
in his capacity as such; and                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(c)    the obligation to observe stipulations relating to foreign exchange set out or               <br /><br /><br />
referred to in Article 26, save in respect of their application to anything done or to              <br /><br /><br />
be done by the Operator in his capacity as such.                                                    <br /><br /><br />
5.3    Eni shall be the Operator. No change of the Operator may take effect unless it has           <br /><br /><br />
been approved in writing by MIREM.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                  Article 6                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                     Commercial Discovery and Development                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
6.1    Where, in the course of the Petroleum Operations, a Discovery of Petroleum is           <br /><br /><br />
made in the EPC Area, the Concessionaire shall as soon as reasonably possible by               <br /><br /><br />
notice inform MIREM whether or not, in its opinion, the said Discovery is of                   <br /><br /><br />
potential commercial interest.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
6.2    For a Discovery of potential commercial interest the Concessionaire shall promptly      <br /><br /><br />
prepare an Appraisal Programme and, after consultation with MIREM, carry out                   <br /><br /><br />
such Appraisal Programme and submit a report of the appraisal activities to                    <br /><br /><br />
MIREM within three (3) months after the completion of the Appraisal Programme.                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
6.3    The Concessionaire shall submit for Government consideration and approval a             <br /><br /><br />
Development Plan for a proposed Development and Production Area for the                        <br /><br /><br />
Discovery, so as to include such a Development and Production Area in a single                 <br /><br /><br />
area, so far as the boundaries of the EPC Area permit, the entire area of the                  <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum reservoir or reservoirs in respect of which a Declaration of                         <br /><br /><br />
Commerciality has been given. MIREM shall consider without undue delay the                     <br /><br /><br />
proposed Development Plan submitted by the Concessionaire. If the MIREM is                     <br /><br /><br />
unable to complete consultation with concerned relevant authorities within twelve              <br /><br /><br />
(12) months from receipt of the proposed Development Plan submitted by the                     <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire for approval, then MIREM shall notify the Concessionaire and shall              <br /><br /><br />
when possible indicate when it is expected that the consultation process shall be              <br /><br /><br />
completed.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
6.4    If Commercial Production of a Discovery has not commenced within a period of            <br /><br /><br />
five years (5) years, or such longer period as may be specified in an approved                 <br /><br /><br />
Development Plan, from the date on which the Development Plan is approved, then                <br /><br /><br />
the rights and obligations of the Concessionaire over the Development and                      <br /><br /><br />
Production Area to which the Discovery relates shall be extinguished as though the             <br /><br /><br />
said area had been surrendered pursuant to Article 29. Such period may be                      <br /><br /><br />
extended:                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />

 months in respect of a portion of the EPC Area so that the area retained,                       <br /><br /><br />
 excluding what is already included in a Development and Production Area                         <br /><br /><br />
 or in a Discovery Area, does not exceed seventy five per cent (75%) of the                      <br /><br /><br />
 EPC Area on the Effective Date;                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    at the commencement of a third Exploration Period of twenty four (24)                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 months in respect of a portion of the EPC Area so that the area retained,                       <br /><br /><br />
 excluding what is already included in a Development and Production Area                         <br /><br /><br />
 or in a Discovery Area, does not exceed seventy five per cent (75%) of the                      <br /><br /><br />
 EPC Area on the Effective Date as reduced under letter (a) above;                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    at the end of the third Exploration Period in respect of the remainder of the            <br /><br /><br />
 EPC Area other than any Development and Production Areas or any area in                         <br /><br /><br />
 respect of which the Exploration Period has been further extended pursuant                      <br /><br /><br />
 to Articles 3.5 (c) and (d).                                                                    <br /><br /><br />

                                   Records and Reports                                        <br /><br /><br />
8.1    The Concessionaire shall prepare and, at all times while this EPC is in force,         <br /><br /><br />

reasonably require.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />

in Article 8.3 or authorised pursuant to Article 23, may not be published,                    <br /><br /><br />
reproduced or otherwise dealt with without the consent of MIREM.                              <br /><br /><br />
8.3    The Concessionaire may retain for its own use copies of material constituting          <br /><br /><br />

material constituting Documentation; provided that samples equivalent in size and             <br /><br /><br />

laboratory' examination or analysis samples or other original materials constituting          <br /><br /><br />
Documentation; provided that samples equivalent in size and quality or, where such            <br /><br /><br />
material is capable of reproduction, copies of equivalent quality have first been             <br /><br /><br />
delivered to MIREM.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />

of activities hereunder during such quarter with plans and maps showing the                   <br /><br /><br />
places where the work described was done; and                                                 <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                          Article 9                                               <br /><br /><br />
                          Cost Recovery and Production Entitlement                                <br /><br /><br />
9.1    The Concessionaire shall bear and pay all costs incurred in carrying out the               <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations in which the Concessionaire participates, and the                            <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire shall recover such costs permitted by the provisions of this EPC                   <br /><br /><br />
including Annex “C” of this EPC (hereinafter “Recoverable Costs”), and shall be                   <br /><br /><br />
remunerated exclusively by means of an entitlement to quantities of Petroleum to                  <br /><br /><br />
which the Concessionaire is entitled as herein provided.                                          <br /><br /><br />
9.2    The provisions related to cost recovery and profit entitlement set out in this Article     <br /><br /><br />
shall apply to Petroleum with effect that the Government and the Concessionaire                   <br /><br /><br />
shall have title in undivided participating entitlement to the Petroleum available for            <br /><br /><br />
sale in any given period. Unless otherwise instructed by Government the sale of                   <br /><br /><br />
such Petroleum shall take place on a joint dedicated basis by the Concessionaire                  <br /><br /><br />
and the Concessionaire will hold those entitlements in undivided proportions equal                <br /><br /><br />
to the proportions in which during that period each Party was entitled to Disposable              <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum. Such instructions shall not affect volumes of Petroleum subject to                     <br /><br /><br />
contract. Accordingly, the proceeds from the sale on a joint dedicated basis of                   <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum in any given period shall be divided between the Government and the                     <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire in the proportions in which they had title in undivided entitlements               <br /><br /><br />
to the Petroleum sold.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
9.3    From the total quantity of Petroleum Produced, the Concessionaire may take a               <br /><br /><br />
portion thereof necessary to discharge the Concessionaire’s obligation for the                    <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Production Tax. The balance of Petroleum remaining after the aforesaid                  <br /><br /><br />
portion has been set aside is hereinafter referred to as “Disposable Petroleum”.                  <br /><br /><br />
9.4    (a) For purposes of the R-factor calculation, Disposable Petroleum and Cost                <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum shall be calculated in respect of the whole of the EPC Area.                            <br /><br /><br />
(b) Insofar as permitted by applicable law and this EPC, all costs incurred by                    <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire in relation to Petroleum Operations shall be recovered from                    <br /><br /><br />
Disposable Petroleum, as available at the Delivery Point.                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 Extent ion copy                                            26                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿ (c) In addition, and in the event the Government and/or the Concessionaire                               <br /><br /><br />
 elect to take Profit Petroleum in kind, the Concessionaire shall, for accounting and                     <br /><br /><br />
 reporting purposes, record Cost Petroleum separately:                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(i)    in respect of each Development and Production Area, and                                            <br /><br /><br />
(ii)    in the form of liquids and gas, on a pro-rata basis relative to the                               <br /><br /><br />
volumes of Petroleum Produced.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
Condensate shall be taken in liquids or gas on the basis of its character at the                          <br /><br /><br />
Delivery Point.                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
9.5    For each calendar year, Cost Petroleum shall be limited to seventy five percent                    <br /><br /><br />
(75%) of Disposable Petroleum.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
9.6    The Cost Petroleum for any quarter calculated in the manner aforesaid shall be                     <br /><br /><br />
increased by:                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(a)    the amount of any contributions made by the Concessionaire into the                                <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Fund during such quarter; and                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(b)    the costs incurred by the Concessionaire during such quarter to implement                          <br /><br /><br />
an approved Decommissioning Plan prepared pursuant to applicable law                                      <br /><br /><br />
and the provisions of Article 15 save to the extent that, such costs have                                 <br /><br /><br />
been funded by withdrawals from the Decommissioning Fund; and                                             <br /><br /><br />
(c)    provided that in no event shall the Cost Petroleum exceed the Disposable                           <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum.                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
9.7    Costs, to the extent permitted by the provisions of Annex “C” of this EPC, shall                   <br /><br /><br />
subject to Article 9.8, be recovered from Cost Petroleum:                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(a) in respect of the amount of Development and Production Capital                                        <br /><br /><br />
Expenditures stipulated in Annex “C” of this EPC incurred during each                                     <br /><br /><br />
year, by the recovery of such amount at a maximum yearly rate of twenty                                   <br /><br /><br />
five (25 %) on a linear depreciation basis, beginning in the year in which                                <br /><br /><br />
Execution copy                               27                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿such amount is incurred or in the calendar year in which Commercial                       <br /><br /><br />
Production commences, whichever year is later;                                            <br /><br /><br />
(b)    in respect of costs attributable to Exploration as stipulated in Annex “C” of      <br /><br /><br />
this EPC (hereinafter referred to as “Exploration Costs”), by the recovery of             <br /><br /><br />
the full amount in the year in which they were incurred or in the year in                 <br /><br /><br />
which Commercial Production commences, whichever year is later; and                       <br /><br /><br />
(c)    in respect of operating costs attributable to Petroleum Operations stipulated      <br /><br /><br />
as Operating Costs in Annex “C” to this EPC (hereinafter referred to as                   <br /><br /><br />
“Operating Costs”) (including any contributions into the Decommissioning                  <br /><br /><br />
Fund pursuant to applicable law, the provisions of Article 15 and including               <br /><br /><br />
any costs incurred by the Concessionaire to implement an approved                         <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Plan prepared pursuant to the provisions of applicable                    <br /><br /><br />
law save to the extent, in either case, that such costs have been funded by               <br /><br /><br />
withdrawals from the Decommissioning Fund), by the recovery of the full                   <br /><br /><br />
amount in the year in which they were incurred.                                           <br /><br /><br />
9.8    To the extent that Recoverable Costs in any year exceed the value of Cost          <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum available in that year, the unrecovered excess shall be carried forward         <br /><br /><br />
for recovery in succeeding years.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
9.9    The quantity of Cost Petroleum to which the Concessionaire is entitled in any year <br /><br /><br />
shall be established on the basis of the value of the Petroleum Produced during           <br /><br /><br />
such year, determined in accordance with Article 10.                                      <br /><br /><br />
9.10    Profit Petroleum, shall be shared between the Government and the Concessionaire   <br /><br /><br />
according to a scale varying with the value of the R-Factor, where:                       <br /><br /><br />
(a)    R-Factor = (Cumulative Cash Inflows) n /                                           <br /><br /><br />
(Cumulative Capital Expenditures) n                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Cumulative Cash Inflows n =                                                        <br /><br /><br />
Cumulative Cash Inflows (n-1)                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                     + Concessionaire portion of Profit Petroleum n                       <br /><br /><br />
Execution copy    28                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
﻿ + Concessionaire’s Cost Petroleum n                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 -    Operating Costs n                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 -    Computed Corporate Income Tax n                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 (c) Cumulative Capital Expenditures n =                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 Cumulative Capital Expenditures (n-1)                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 + Exploration Costs n                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 + Development and Production Capital Expenditures n                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Where:                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
n is the current year; and (n-1) is the previous year;                                   <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire’s Cost Petroleum is the amount of Recoverable Costs                       <br /><br /><br />
actually recovered;                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
Computed Corporate Income Tax is the Concessionaire’s corporate income                   <br /><br /><br />
tax obligation computed according to applicable tax law and Article 11.                  <br /><br /><br />
For the purpose of calculating the R-Factor, the first year (n=l) shall be the year      <br /><br /><br />
during which the Effective Date occurs. Any Capital Expenditures incurred prior to       <br /><br /><br />
the Effective Date shall not be deemed for the purpose of the R-Factor calculation       <br /><br /><br />
to have been incurred during the year of the Effective Date.                             <br /><br /><br />
The R-Factor shall be calculated on the last day of each calendar year and the           <br /><br /><br />
applicable ratio shall determine the sharing of Profit Petroleum throughout the          <br /><br /><br />
following calendar year.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />

9.11    (a) If there is a breach of the warranty set out in Article 11.6 or in the event that                   <br /><br /><br />
after the Effective Date there is a change in the laws of the Republic of                                       <br /><br /><br />
Mozambique of the kind referred to in Article 11 and as a result the Parties                                    <br /><br /><br />
meet to agree on changes to be made to this EPC, then during the period                                         <br /><br /><br />
starting when the change in the law comes into effect and ending when an                                        <br /><br /><br />
agreement between the Parties is reached pursuant to Article 11, the portion of                                 <br /><br /><br />
Profit Petroleum to which the Concessionaire and the Government would                                           <br /><br /><br />
otherwise be entitled shall be adjusted so that the net revenues to be received by                              <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire from Petroleum Operations are the same as they would have                                    <br /><br /><br />
been if no change in the law had taken place.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
(b) Where the Parties have reached agreement on the changes to be made to this                                  <br /><br /><br />
EPC pursuant to Article 11, this EPC will be deemed to stand amended to the                                     <br /><br /><br />
extent necessary to give effect to that agreement in accordance with its terms.                                 <br /><br /><br />
9.12 Concessionaire’s Cost Petroleum and Profit Petroleum calculations shall be done                            <br /><br /><br />
for each calendar year on an accumulative basis. To the extent that actual quantities                           <br /><br /><br />
and expenses are not known, provisional estimates based on the approved work                                    <br /><br /><br />
programme and operating and capital budgets shall be used. Until such time as the                               <br /><br /><br />
value of Petroleum attributable to a year is determined, the calculations will be                               <br /><br /><br />
based on the value of such Petroleum during the preceding year and in the absence                               <br /><br /><br />
of such value, on the value agreed to between MIREM and the Concessionaire.                                     <br /><br /><br />
Adjustments shall be made during the succeeding year based on actual Petroleum                                  <br /><br /><br />
quantities, prices and expenses in relation to such year.                                                       <br /><br /><br />

﻿ 9.13 Any person constituting the Concessionaire, excluding an entity holding a State     <br /><br /><br />
Participating Interest or a Permitted Assignee, shall pay all costs properly incurred     <br /><br /><br />
under this EPC in relation to the State Participating Interest (herein referred to as     <br /><br /><br />
“Carry”) subject to the following conditions:                                             <br /><br /><br />
a)    Carry shall be paid by Concessionaires having a Carry obligation pro-rata to        <br /><br /><br />
their Participating Interests in this EPC.                                                <br /><br /><br />
b)    In the event that a third party, other than an entity holding a State               <br /><br /><br />
Participating Interest or a Permitted Assignee, has acquired a Participating              <br /><br /><br />
Interest in the EPC from any person constituting the Concessionaire, such                 <br /><br /><br />
third party shall be obliged to take over a proportionate share of the Carry.             <br /><br /><br />
c)    If a State Participating Interest is totally or partially transferred to a non-     <br /><br /><br />
Permitted Assignee, the Carry already paid with respect to the transferred                <br /><br /><br />
interest and not yet reimbursed to the Concessionaires subject to Cany shall              <br /><br /><br />
be immediately due and paid to the Concessionaires pro-rata to their                      <br /><br /><br />
respective Participating Interests by such non-Permitted Assignee. The share              <br /><br /><br />
of any future Carry, to be borne by each Concessionaire having a Carry                    <br /><br /><br />
obligation, shall be calculated according to the new composition of the                   <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaires having such Carry obligation.                                             <br /><br /><br />
d)    The Carry shall be limited to all costs incurred under this EPC by the              <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire in discharging its obligations under this EPC, up to and                   <br /><br /><br />
including the date upon which the Development Plan has been approved.                     <br /><br /><br />
e)    The Cany shall be used exclusively to pay for costs properly incurred under         <br /><br /><br />
this EPC in relation to the State Participating Interest. Save for in respect of a        <br /><br /><br />
transfer to a Permitted Assignee, ENH may not assign directly or indirectly               <br /><br /><br />
the benefits derived under Carry. Any transfer of a Participating Interest                <br /><br /><br />
subject to Carry requires the prior written approval of MIREM. The term                   <br /><br /><br />
“Permitted Assignee” means for the purpose of this Article the Government                 <br /><br /><br />
or a Mozambican Person wholly owned and controlled by the Government.                     <br /><br /><br />

﻿Article 10                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
Valuation of Petroleum                                                               <br /><br /><br />
The value of Petroleum referred to in Articles 9 and 11 shall, to the extent such    <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum consists of Crude Oil, be determined at the end of each calendar month     <br /><br /><br />
commencing with the calendar month in which Commercial Production of Crude           <br /><br /><br />
Oil begins. To the extent such Petroleum consists of Natural Gas it shall be         <br /><br /><br />
determined at the end of each calendar month commencing with the calendar            <br /><br /><br />
month in which commercial delivery at the Delivery Point begins.                     <br /><br /><br />
A value for each separate export grade of Crude Oil will be:                         <br /><br /><br />
(a)    in the case of sales to non-Affiliated Companies, the weighted average price  <br /><br /><br />
per barrel at the Delivery Point of each separate export grade of Crude Oil          <br /><br /><br />
being the prices FOB within the meaning defined in Incoterms 2000, at                <br /><br /><br />
which such Crude Oil has been sold by the Concessionaire during that                 <br /><br /><br />
calendar month; or                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
(b)    If the Concessionaire sells the Crude Oil to a third party on terms different <br /><br /><br />
from FOB (as per Incoterms 2000), then for the purpose of this EPC, a                <br /><br /><br />
calculated net-back FOB price shall be applied. The net-back FOB price               <br /><br /><br />
shall be established by deducting from the price agreed the actual and direct        <br /><br /><br />
costs incurred by the Concessionaire in fulfilling the obligations under their       <br /><br /><br />
sales contract additional to those obligations included under a FOB contract.        <br /><br /><br />
(c)    in the case of sales to Affiliated Companies, such price as agreed between    <br /><br /><br />
MIREM and the Concessionaire on the basis of adding the following two                <br /><br /><br />
factors together:                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(i) the weighted average calendar month FOB price for Brent rated Crude              <br /><br /><br />
Oil, or such other appropriate marker Crude Oil for the production in                <br /><br /><br />
question for the period in question. The weighted average will be                    <br /><br /><br />
based on the days in each calendar month when a closing price is                     <br /><br /><br />
reported in Platts Oilgram price report. Days such as weekends and                   <br /><br /><br />
holidays with no price reports will be ignored;                                      <br /><br /><br />
﻿(ii) a premium or discount to the price of the Brent rated Crude Oil, or           <br /><br /><br />
such other appropriate marker Crude Oil for the production in                      <br /><br /><br />
question to be determined by reference to the quality of the Crude Oil             <br /><br /><br />
produced from the EPC Area and the cost of moving such Crude Oil                   <br /><br /><br />
to the market.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
10.3 In any case in which MIREM and the Concessionaire are unable to agree a price <br /><br /><br />
 under Article 10.2 (c), in order to determine the premium or discount referred to <br /><br /><br />
therein the following procedures shall be undertaken:                              <br /><br /><br />
(a)    MIREM and the Concessionaire shall submit to each other their assessments   <br /><br /><br />
of the premium or discount together with an explanation of the key factors         <br /><br /><br />
taken into consideration in assessing the premium or discount;                     <br /><br /><br />
(b)    if the premium or discount submitted by each of MIREM and the               <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire are within ten United States Cents (10 US 0) per barrel of          <br /><br /><br />
each other the average will be taken for the purposes of setting the final         <br /><br /><br />
value of the Crude Oil;                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(c)    if the premium or discount submitted by each of MIREM and the               <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire differ by more than ten United States Cents (10 US 0) per           <br /><br /><br />
barrel each will resubmit a revised premium or discount to the other on the        <br /><br /><br />
third (3rd) business day after the first exchange of information;                  <br /><br /><br />
(d)    if the premium or discount submitted by each of MIREM and the               <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire on the second exchange of information are within ten                <br /><br /><br />
United States Cents (10 US 0) per barrel of each other the average will be         <br /><br /><br />
taken for the purposes of setting the final value of Crude Oil;                    <br /><br /><br />
(e)    if the premium or discount submitted on the second exchange of              <br /><br /><br />
information differ by more than ten United States Cents (10 US 0) per              <br /><br /><br />
barrel the matter shall, in accordance with Article 30.6, be referred for          <br /><br /><br />
determination by a sole expert who shall establish a price based on the            <br /><br /><br />
criteria set out in Article 10.2(c) but always within the range established by     <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                               the Parties under Article 10.3(d).                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
10.4 The value calculated for Natural Gas Produced from reservoirs within the EPC                <br /><br /><br />
Area shall be:                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
(a)    in the case of sales to non-Affiliated Companies, the weighted average price              <br /><br /><br />
per Gigajoule of commercial specification Natural Gas at the Delivery Point                      <br /><br /><br />
at which such Natural Gas has been delivered by the Concessionaire during                        <br /><br /><br />
that calendar month, shall be the weighted average price per Gigajoule of all                    <br /><br /><br />
other commercial specification Natural Gas delivered during the same                             <br /><br /><br />
calendar month from reservoirs subject to the jurisdiction of the Republic of                    <br /><br /><br />
Mozambique and the weighted average of posted or publicly available                              <br /><br /><br />
prices for alternative fuels to Natural Gas for large scale industrial                           <br /><br /><br />
consumers including power generators in the market where such has been                           <br /><br /><br />
delivered to ultimate customers.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(b)    in the case of sales to Affiliated Companies, such price as stipulated in sub-            <br /><br /><br />
paragraph a) above for sales to non-Affiliated Companies or such price                           <br /><br /><br />
agreed between MIREM and the Concessionaire.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
10.5. In the event that the Government enters into a commercial Gas and/or Crude Oil             <br /><br /><br />
Sales Agreement with the Concessionaire for the purchase by the Government of                    <br /><br /><br />
Crude Oil and/or Natural Gas from the Concessionaire, such sales shall be at a                   <br /><br /><br />
price no higher than the price of Crude Oil and/or Natural Gas sold to Affiliated                <br /><br /><br />
Companies from the EPC Area as determined in terms of this Article 10.                           <br /><br /><br />

﻿                     Article 11                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                              Fiscal Terms and Other Charges                                  <br /><br /><br />
11.1    The Concessionaire and its Subcontractors shall, save to the extent they are exempt   <br /><br /><br />
therefrom, be subject to all applicable law of the Republic of Mozambique which               <br /><br /><br />
impose taxes, duties, levies, charges, fees or contributions.                                 <br /><br /><br />
11.2    During the term of this EPC, the Concessionaire and its Subcontractors are entitled   <br /><br /><br />
to the rights of Tax and Customs Incentives in terms of Law No. 3/2001, of 21                 <br /><br /><br />
February as defined in the Code of Fiscal Benefits (CFB), approved by Decree No.              <br /><br /><br />
16/2002, of 27 June. The Concessionaire and its Subcontractors shall be exempt                <br /><br /><br />
from the payment of the following taxes, duties, imposts, and other charges:                  <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Customs duties with regard to the importation of goods destined to be used             <br /><br /><br />
in Petroleum Operations, vehicles and other imported supplies, but                            <br /><br /><br />
excluding light vehicles for transport of passengers in accordance with                       <br /><br /><br />
article 44 paragraph a) of the CFB;                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Duties and other customs and fiscal charges on goods temporarily imported              <br /><br /><br />
for use in Petroleum Operations, including but not limited to such as                         <br /><br /><br />
drilling rigs, seismic vessels, machinery, equipment, aircraft and boats in                   <br /><br /><br />
accordance with article 44 paragraph b) of the CFB;                                           <br /><br /><br />
(c)    Customs duties on the exportation of the goods referred to in the preceding            <br /><br /><br />
paragraphs once the goods no longer are needed for the Petroleum                              <br /><br /><br />
Operations in accordance with article 44 paragraph c) of the CFB;                             <br /><br /><br />
(d)    Customs duties and custom charges with regard to the exportation of                    <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Produced in the Republic of Mozambique in accordance with                           <br /><br /><br />
article 44 paragraph d) of the CFB; and                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(e)    The imports and exports referred to in the preceding paragraphs shall also             <br /><br /><br />
benefit from an exemption from the Value Added Tax (VAT) as provided                          <br /><br /><br />
in the VAT Code approved by Decree No. 51/98, of 29 September in                              <br /><br /><br />
accordance with article 44 paragraph e) of the CFB.                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿11.3 The Expatriate Personnel of the Concessionaire and of its Subcontractors shall be                                               <br /><br /><br />
exempt under this EPC from:                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Any and all taxes on or related to the income of non resident Expatriate                                                      <br /><br /><br />
Personnel of the Concessionaire or its Subcontractors or any other tax of a                                                          <br /><br /><br />
similar nature imposed on the work earnings of such Expatriate Personnel;                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Customs duties and other levies payable on the importation of personal and                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                        household effects of Expatriate Personnel and their dependants imported                      <br /><br /><br />
                                        into the Republic of Mozambique on first arrival, provided that those                        <br /><br /><br />
                                        customs duties shall become payable on such items upon their sale in the                     <br /><br /><br />
                                        Republic of Mozambique to a person who is not exempt from such duties.                       <br /><br /><br />
                                        The Expatriate Personnel shall have the right to export from the Republic of                 <br /><br /><br />
                                        Mozambique free of any customs duties and levies the aforesaid personal                      <br /><br /><br />
                                        and household effects imported by them, within the conditions stipulated in                  <br /><br /><br />
                                        the customs tariff.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                           Article 13                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                     Lifting Arrangements                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
13.1    (a) The Concessionaire shall subject to provisions regulating the production              <br /><br /><br />
and sale of Petroleum be entitled to lift and export freely its entitlement to                    <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Produced under this EPC.                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Each Party shall take its entitlement to Petroleum consistent with Good                    <br /><br /><br />
Oilfield Practice at an approximately regular rate throughout each calendar                       <br /><br /><br />
year.                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(c)    Not later than ninety (90) days prior to the date scheduled for the                        <br /><br /><br />
commencement of Commercial Production, the Parties shall establish                                <br /><br /><br />
offtake procedures covering the scheduling, storage and lifting of Petroleum                      <br /><br /><br />
and such other matters as the Parties shall agree. Such procedures shall be                       <br /><br /><br />
consistent with Good Oilfield Practice.                                                           <br /><br /><br />
13.2    Notwithstanding Article 9.2 or instructions given in accordance with Article 9.2,         <br /><br /><br />
the Government may by six (6) months notice given to the Concessionaire or                        <br /><br /><br />
Operator require the Concessionaire or Operator to sell on behalf of the                          <br /><br /><br />
Government during the succeeding calendar year unless otherwise instructed the                    <br /><br /><br />
whole or any portion of the volume of Petroleum Production Tax taken in kind and                  <br /><br /><br />
when applicable Profit Petroleum not previously committed to which the                            <br /><br /><br />
Government is entitled pursuant to this EPC during said succeeding year. The                      <br /><br /><br />
quantity of such Profit Petroleum, which the Government desires to sell shall be                  <br /><br /><br />
specified in said notice. The Concessionaire or Operator shall sell that quantity of              <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum on the open market at the best price reasonably obtainable and remit the                <br /><br /><br />
proceeds of the sale directly and forthwith to the Government. The Concessionaire                 <br /><br /><br />
or Operator shall not charge the Government any fee for the selling of the                        <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum of the Government.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                          Article 14                              <br /><br /><br />
                     Conservation of Petroleum and Prevention of Loss                             <br /><br /><br />
14.1    The Concessionaire shall, before carrying out any drilling, prepare and submit for        <br /><br /><br />
review by MIREM a well programme including a contingency plan designed to                         <br /><br /><br />
achieve rapid and effective emergency response in the event of a blow-out or fire,                <br /><br /><br />
escape, waste or loss of Petroleum or damage to Petroleum bearing strata.                         <br /><br /><br />
14.2    In the event of a blow-out or fire, escape, waste or loss of Petroleum or damage to       <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum bearing strata, the Concessionaire shall notify MIREM within twenty                     <br /><br /><br />
four (24) hours of becoming aware of such occurrence, promptly implement the                      <br /><br /><br />
relevant contingency plan and as soon as practicable thereafter submit a full report              <br /><br /><br />
thereon to MIREM.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
14.3    Without prejudice to the obligations of the Concessionaire under Article 29, in the       <br /><br /><br />
case of relinquishment or surrender by the Concessionaire or termination of the                   <br /><br /><br />
rights of the Concessionaire pursuant to this EPC, the Concessionaire shall within                <br /><br /><br />
ninety (90) days from the date of such relinquishment, surrender or termination, in               <br /><br /><br />
respect of the whole of the EPC Area or, as the case may be, any part of the EPC                  <br /><br /><br />
Area which has been relinquished or surrendered:                                                  <br /><br /><br />
a) plug or close off, in a manner consistent with Good Oilfield Practice, all                     <br /><br /><br />
wells drilled as part of the Petroleum Operations unless otherwise agreed                         <br /><br /><br />
between MIREM and the Concessionaire.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(b) take all action necessary, in accordance with Good Oilfield Practice, to                      <br /><br /><br />
prevent hazards to human life or to the property of others or the                                 <br /><br /><br />
environment resulting from conditions in the EPC Area or, as the case may                         <br /><br /><br />
be, any part thereof caused by Petroleum Operations, being conditions                             <br /><br /><br />
which were or ought with reasonable diligence to have been evident at the                         <br /><br /><br />
time of relinquishment, surrender or termination.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
