﻿                        Article 15                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                  Decommissioning                                       <br /><br /><br />
15.1 If in the reasonable expectation of the Concessionaire, the Concessionaire will    <br /><br /><br />
cease to produce Petroleum under this EPC from the EPC Area, the EPC expires,           <br /><br /><br />
is cancelled or surrendered pursuant to the proceedure stipulated in this EPC and       <br /><br /><br />
applicable law the Concessionaire shall submit to MIREM for approval a                  <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Plan. The Decommissioning Plan shall be prepared in                     <br /><br /><br />
accordance with applicable law and shall include, but not be limited to:                <br /><br /><br />
(a)    particulars, separately set out in respect of each Development and               <br /><br /><br />
Production Area, of measures to be taken, to effect decommissioning                     <br /><br /><br />
including but not limited to:                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(i)    decommissioning of equipment and installations for each                          <br /><br /><br />
Development and Production Area;                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(ii)    timely removal of equipment and installations not required for                  <br /><br /><br />
ongoing Petroleum Operations in any other Development and                               <br /><br /><br />
Production Area; and                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(iii)    any other steps that may reasonably be required in order to prevent            <br /><br /><br />
hazard to human life, or to the property of others or to the                            <br /><br /><br />
environment.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(b)    estimates of the time required to complete operations under the plan;            <br /><br /><br />
(c)    a budget for operations under the plan, including particulars of the costs of    <br /><br /><br />
decommissioning equipment and installations;                                            <br /><br /><br />
(d)    a schedule of the work programme with related costs to be drawn from the         <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Fund in order to meet the costs of implementing the plan;               <br /><br /><br />
and                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(e)    such environmental, engineering and feasibility studies as may be necessary      <br /><br /><br />
to support the proposed plan.                                                           <br /><br /><br />
   15.2 The Decommissioning Plan shall be prepared in compliance with applicable law    <br /><br /><br />
           and the provisions of Article 28 and shall ensure that decommissioning is    <br /><br /><br />
Ksccutton copy    48                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿conducted in a manner which will give effect to standards generally recognised as           <br /><br /><br />
applicable in the international petroleum industry and the Concessionaire’s                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
standards for decommissioning.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
15.3    In the event that the Concessionaire does not submit a Decommissioning Plan to      <br /><br /><br />
MIREM within the time allowed MIREM may serve upon the Concessionaire a                     <br /><br /><br />
notice requiring the Concessionaire to submit to MIREM, within a period of ninety           <br /><br /><br />
(90) days from date on which the notice was served, a Decommissioning Plan. If              <br /><br /><br />
within that period no Decommissioning Plan is submitted, MIREM may                          <br /><br /><br />
commission consultants of international standing to prepare a Decommissioning               <br /><br /><br />
Plan.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
15.4    A Decommissioning Plan prepared by a consultant in accordance with applicable       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
law and this Article shall be implemented by the Concessionaire in accordance with          <br /><br /><br />
its terms as though it were an obligation of the Concessionaire set forth in Article        <br /><br /><br />
28. The cost of commissioning engineering consultants to prepare a consultant’s             <br /><br /><br />
plan shall be payable by the Concessionaire to the Government.                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
15.5    In the event that the Concessionaire considers that production from a Development   <br /><br /><br />
and Production Area will cease before a Decommissioning Plan has been prepared,             <br /><br /><br />
decommissioning measures for that Development and Production Area will be                   <br /><br /><br />
prepared by the Concessionaire in accordance with the requirement for                       <br /><br /><br />
decommissioning set out in Articles 15.3 and 15.4, and where those measures have            <br /><br /><br />
been approved by MIREM will take effect as an amendment to the Development                  <br /><br /><br />
Plan for that Development and Production Area.                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
15.6 Not later than at the commencement of Petroleum production from reserves within        <br /><br /><br />
the EPC Area, the Concessionaire shall establish in a bank of its choice an interest        <br /><br /><br />
bearing United States dollar account or such other currency account to be mutually          <br /><br /><br />
agreed by the Parties to be denominated as the Decommissioning Fund into which              <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire shall set aside from time to time funds to be able to cover the          <br /><br /><br />
decommissioning costs calculated in accordance with this EPC to meet the                    <br /><br /><br />
estimated costs of implementing an approved Decommissioning Plan. At the time               <br /><br /><br />
of establishment of the account for the Decommissioning Fund the Concessioaire              <br /><br /><br />
shall deposit US dollars ten thousand (US$ 10.000) or equivalent amount if an               <br /><br /><br />
Execution copy    49    ft    t X'                                                          <br /><br /><br />
﻿alternative currency is agreed. The bank so designated shall have a long term rating           <br /><br /><br />
of not less than “AA” by Standard and Poor’s Corporation or “Aa2” by Moody’s                   <br /><br /><br />
Investor Service or a comparable rating by another mutually agreed rating service.             <br /><br /><br />
Preference shall be given to banks in Mozambique possessing the required rating.               <br /><br /><br />
15.7 The calculation of the amounts to be set aside for estimated future                       <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning costs into the Decommissioning Fund shall be governed as                       <br /><br /><br />
follows:                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
a)    The estimates of: (i) the recoverable reserves and the projected production schedule     <br /><br /><br />
and (ii) total decommissioning costs for the Concessionaire proposed                           <br /><br /><br />
decommissioning solution as well as reasonable alternative decommissioning                     <br /><br /><br />
solutions shall be submitted for MIREM approval. The M1REM shall based on the                  <br /><br /><br />
proposals from the Concessionaire select a preliminary decommissioning solution                <br /><br /><br />
to form the basis for the calculation of decommissioning costs to be covered by a              <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Fund created for the purpose of covering such decommissioning                  <br /><br /><br />
costs. Adequate provisions for successive revisions of such estimates shall when               <br /><br /><br />
required herein, required by applicable law or deemed necessary by the                         <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire due to substantial changes in fact also be included in any updated              <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Plan.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
b)    In any calendar year in which the Concessionaire did not submit to MIREM a               <br /><br /><br />
revised Decommissioning Plan or the total estimated decommissioning cost,                      <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire shall update the value of the latest total estimated decommissioning            <br /><br /><br />
cost preliminary approved by MIREM in order to account for the escalation of such              <br /><br /><br />
approved estimated decommissioning costs in the period between the calendar year               <br /><br /><br />
in which such costs were estimated and the then current calendar year. For this                <br /><br /><br />
purpose, and for each calendar year, the applicable annual US Dollar escalation                <br /><br /><br />
index shall be based on the Producers Price Index for the Drilling of Oil and Gas              <br /><br /><br />
Wells as published by the United States Bureau of Labor Statistics The annual                  <br /><br /><br />
index to be used in year “n” shall be determined by difference between the annual              <br /><br /><br />
index relating to the year in which the latest approved estimate is determined and             <br /><br /><br />
the same annual index relating such year “n”. In the event the above US Bureau of              <br /><br /><br />
Labour Statistic ceases, for any reason whatsoever, to publish the Producers Price             <br /><br /><br />
Index for the Drilling of Oil and Gas Wells set out in the preceding paragraph of              <br /><br /><br />
 •vmitlon cupv                                         50                                      <br /><br /><br />
﻿this Clause or when an alternative currency is selected, Parties shall determine               <br /><br /><br />
either an alternative independent internationally recognised source, or an alternative         <br /><br /><br />
representative index.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
15.8    The Concessionaire will not withdraw money from the Decommissioning Fund               <br /><br /><br />
save for the purpose of meeting the costs of implementing an approved                          <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Plan and all statements relating to the Decommissioning Fund                   <br /><br /><br />
provided by the bank from time to time shall be copied to MIREM.                               <br /><br /><br />
15.9    Payments into the Decommissioning Fund shall be cost recoverable in accordance         <br /><br /><br />
with provisions applicable to this EPC.                                                        <br /><br /><br />
15.10    Costs incurred by the Concessionaire to implement an approved Decommissioning         <br /><br /><br />
Plan shall be cost recoverable in accordance with provisions in that regard set out in         <br /><br /><br />
Article 9 and for the purpose of IRPC shall be treated as an operating expense save            <br /><br /><br />
where, in either case, such costs have been funded by withdrawals from the                     <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Fund.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
15.11    Any funds remaining in the Decommissioning Fund after the approved                    <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Plan has been completed shall be treated as Profit Petroleum and               <br /><br /><br />
the remaining balance shall be shared in accordance with the provision of Article              <br /><br /><br />
9.7.                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
15.12    In the event that at the time of implementing any Decommissioning Plan there are      <br /><br /><br />
insufficient funds available in the Decommissioning Fund to fund the operations of             <br /><br /><br />
that plan, the shortfall shall be met in full by the Concessionaire.                           <br /><br /><br />
15.13    An approved Decommissioning Plan shall, subject to the provisions of Article 20.2,    <br /><br /><br />
be implemented prudently and without undue delay.                                              <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                          Article 16                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                          Insurance                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
16.1 The Concessionaire shall effect and maintain, in respect of Petroleum Operations,                          <br /><br /><br />
unless otherwise agreed between the Parties, all insurance required by applicable                               <br /><br /><br />
Mozambican law and, as the case may be, required by other applicable law and                                    <br /><br /><br />
such other insurance as MIREM and the Concessionaire may agree from time to                                     <br /><br /><br />
time. Such insurance shall at least include insurance against the following risks:                              <br /><br /><br />
(a)    loss or damage to all Installations and equipment which are owned or used                                <br /><br /><br />
by the Concessionaire in the Petroleum Operations;                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(b)    pollution caused in the course of the Petroleum Operations by the                                        <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire for which the Concessionaire may be held responsible;                                            <br /><br /><br />
(c)    property loss or damage or bodily injury suffered by any third party in the                              <br /><br /><br />
course of the Petroleum Operations by the Concessionaire for which the                                          <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire may be liable to indemnify the Government;                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(d)    the cost of removing wrecks and cleaning up operations following an                                      <br /><br /><br />
accident in the course of the Petroleum Operations by the Concessionaire;                                       <br /><br /><br />
and                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(e)    the Concessionaire’s and/or the Operator’s liability for its employees                                   <br /><br /><br />
engaged in the Petroleum Operations.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 16.2 In relation to Development and Production Operations, the Concessionaire shall                            <br /><br /><br />
 submit to MIREM a programme for the provision of an “All Risks” insurance                                      <br /><br /><br />
 which may, inter alia, cover physical damage to the facilities under construction                              <br /><br /><br />
 and installation as well as legal liabilities arising out of the Development and                               <br /><br /><br />
 Production Operations.                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 16.3                      Any insurance required to be effected by the Concessionaire pursuant to the          <br /><br /><br />
                           provision of Articles 16.1 and 16.2 may, at the Concessionaire’s discretion and      <br /><br /><br />
                           subject to the approval of MIREM, be provided by one or more of the following        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 Kxi'cution copy                                                       52                                       <br /><br /><br />
﻿ options:                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(a)    non-insurance wherein the Concessionaire itself carries the risks and no                <br /><br /><br />
premia are charged; provided, however, that in the case of any losses or                       <br /><br /><br />
damages resulting from a risk where the Concessionaire has elected to non-                     <br /><br /><br />
insure, such losses or damages shall not be Recoverable Costs for the                          <br /><br /><br />
purpose of Annex “C” of this EPC;                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(b)    insurance through an insurance company wholly owned by the Operator or                  <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire in which case the premia charged shall be at prevailing                     <br /><br /><br />
international insurance market rates;                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(c)    the Concessionaire utilising for the benefit of Petroleum Operations                    <br /><br /><br />
insurance which is placed as part of a global coverage in which case the                       <br /><br /><br />
premia charged shall be at the rates obtained for such global coverage; or                     <br /><br /><br />
(d)    subject to Article 19, insurance through the international insurance markets            <br /><br /><br />
at prevailing rates, provided that:                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(i)    an insurance company wholly owned by the Operator or a                                  <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire may participate in any internationally placed                                   <br /><br /><br />
insurance or reinsurance; and                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
(ii)    the Concessionaire shall have the option to tender and effect all                      <br /><br /><br />
appropriate reinsurance for any insurance placed through insurance                             <br /><br /><br />
companies registered in the Republic of Mozambique.                                            <br /><br /><br />
16.4    Unless otherwise approved by M1REM, the Concessionaire shall competitively             <br /><br /><br />
tender all renewable insurances placed into the international markets at least once            <br /><br /><br />
every three (3) years.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
16.5    The Concessionaire shall require its Subcontractors to carry equivalent insurance of   <br /><br /><br />
the type and in such amount as is required by law and is customary in the                      <br /><br /><br />
international petroleum industry in accordance with Good Oilfield Practice.                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                                            Article 17                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                         Natural Gas                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
17.1    The Concessionaire shall have the right to use Natural Gas extracted from                                             <br /><br /><br />
reservoirs within the EPC Area for the Petroleum Operations in the EPC Area                                                   <br /><br /><br />
including but not limited to power generation, pressure maintenance and recycling                                             <br /><br /><br />
operations.                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
17.2    The terms and conditions relating to the use and production of Associated Natural                                     <br /><br /><br />
Gas shall be as follows:                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(a)    In the event the Concessionaire elects to process and sell Associated Natural                                          <br /><br /><br />
Gas, the Concessionaire shall notify MIREM and, for the purposes of cost                                                      <br /><br /><br />
recovery and entitlement of production, such Natural Gas shall be treated by                                                  <br /><br /><br />
the Parties in the same way as other Natural Gas.                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(b)    In the event the Concessionaire elects not to process and sell Associated                                              <br /><br /><br />
Natural Gas not used for purposes stipulated in Article 17.1 or paragraph (c)                                                 <br /><br /><br />
below, the Government may offtake without any payment to the                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire but at the Government’s sole risk and cost, such Natural Gas                                                   <br /><br /><br />
at the gas/oil separator; provided that such offtake does not materially                                                      <br /><br /><br />
disrupt or delay the conduct of the Petroleum Operations.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(c)    The Concessionaire may re-inject any Associated Natural Gas which is not                                               <br /><br /><br />
taken by Government pursuant to paragraph (b) above, used for Petroleum                                                       <br /><br /><br />
Operations, processed and sold by the Concessionaire, or taken by                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                         Government in accordance with paragraph (b) above, and the costs of such             <br /><br /><br />
                                         disposal shall be recoverable to the extent that such re-injection is included       <br /><br /><br />
                                         in the Development Plan.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 17.3 The terms and conditions relating to the Appraisal Program and the commercial                                           <br /><br /><br />
 assessment of the production and sale of non-Associated Natural Gas shall be as                                              <br /><br /><br />
 follows:                                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (a) On completion of an Appraisal Programme relating to a Discovery of non-                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 li'xccution copy                                                           54                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿Associated Natural Gas made by the Concessionaire and the submission of                                  <br /><br /><br />
an appraisal report thereon, the “Commercial Assessment Period” shall, if                                <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire so requests, commence and shall continue in respect of                                <br /><br /><br />
any Discovery Area for a period of six (6) years, exercisable at the sole                                <br /><br /><br />
option of the Concessionaire. An extension may be granted upon                                           <br /><br /><br />
application by the Concessionaire to the Government, for a second period of                              <br /><br /><br />
up to two (2) years. An appraisal report submitted under this Article shall                              <br /><br /><br />
include the estimated recoverable reserves, projects delivery rate and                                   <br /><br /><br />
pressure, quality specifications and other technical and economic factors                                <br /><br /><br />
relevant to the determination of a market for available Natural Gas. The                                 <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire may, at any time during the Commercial Assessment                                         <br /><br /><br />
Period, inform the MIREM by notice that the Petroleum reservoir located                                  <br /><br /><br />
in any Discovery of non-Associated Natural Gas made by the                                               <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire in respect of which an appraisal report has been submitted,                               <br /><br /><br />
is commercial.                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(b) If the Concessionaire does not request a Commercial Assessment Period                                <br /><br /><br />
pursuant to paragraph (a) above within ninety (90) days from the date on                                 <br /><br /><br />
which the appraisal report was submitted, the Concessionaire shall inform                                <br /><br /><br />
the MIREM by notice whether any Discovery of non-Associated Natural                                      <br /><br /><br />
Gas made by the Concessionaire in respect of which an appraisal report has                               <br /><br /><br />
been submitted, is commercial.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
Where the Concessionaire pursuant to this Article gives notice that any Discovery of                     <br /><br /><br />
non-Associated Natural Gas made by the Concessionaire is commercial, that notice                         <br /><br /><br />
shall, for the purpose of this EPC, be a notice of Commercial Discovery.                                 <br /><br /><br />
17.4 The Commercial Assessment Period shall end on the first to occur of:                                <br /><br /><br />
(a)    the date following that on which Concessionaire gives a Notice of                                 <br /><br /><br />
Commercial Discovery under Article 17.3;                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(b)    the date that the Concessionaire voluntarily surrenders the Discovery Area                        <br /><br /><br />
                                    to which the Commercial Assessment Period relates; or                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />

﻿(c) expiry of the period to which Concessionaire is entitled to under Article                       <br /><br /><br />
17.3.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
17.5    The Concessionaire shall be deemed to have relinquished all rights to the Discovery         <br /><br /><br />
of non-Associated Natural Gas if it has not given a notice of Commercial                            <br /><br /><br />
Discovery under Article 17.3 by the end of the Commercial Assessment Period or                      <br /><br /><br />
on earlier relinquishment of that portion of the EPC Area.                                          <br /><br /><br />
17.6    The Concessionaire shall be responsible for investigating market opportunities and          <br /><br /><br />
seek to develop a market for non-Associated Natural Gas produced from any                           <br /><br /><br />
Development and Production Area and shall sell such non-Associated Natural Gas                      <br /><br /><br />
on a joint dedicated basis on terms common to all the parties constituting the                      <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire. Every contract for the sale of such non-Associated Natural Gas                      <br /><br /><br />
made by the Concessionaire under this article shall be subject to approval by the                   <br /><br /><br />
MIREM. In applying for such approval the Concessionaire shall demonstrate to the                    <br /><br /><br />
MIREM that the prices and other terms of sale of such Natural Gas represents the                    <br /><br /><br />
market value obtainable for such Natural Gas, taking into consideration a fair                      <br /><br /><br />
market cost for transporting the Natural Gas from the Delivery Point to the                         <br /><br /><br />
purchaser and having regard to the alternative uses and markets that can be                         <br /><br /><br />
developed for such Natural Gas.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
17.7    With its application for approval of any gas sales contract, pursuant to Article 17.6,      <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire may apply in respect of any Development and Production Area                      <br /><br /><br />
from which non-Associated Natural Gas will be produced for sale under that gas                      <br /><br /><br />
sales contract, for an extension of the Development and Production Period and                       <br /><br /><br />
where such extension is necessary to facilitate the sale of gas under any such                      <br /><br /><br />
contract the MIREM will grant the same.                                                             <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                                          Article 18                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                           Employment and Training                                                   <br /><br /><br />
18.1 Subject to the Government’s security review of any individual entering                                          <br /><br /><br />
Mozambique and the procedures and formalities of the applicable Mozambican law                                       <br /><br /><br />
relating to immigration the Government shall provide the necessary permits or                                        <br /><br /><br />
other approvals required for the employment and admission into the Republic of                                       <br /><br /><br />
Mozambique of Expatriate Personnel employed by the Concessionaire or its                                             <br /><br /><br />
Subcontractors for the purpose of this EPC.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
18.2    In the conduct of the Petroleum Operations, the Concessionaire shall endeavour to                            <br /><br /><br />
utilise citizens of the Republic of Mozambique having appropriate qualifications to                                  <br /><br /><br />
the maximum extent possible at all levels of its organisation, as Sub-Contractors or                                 <br /><br /><br />
employed by Sub-Contractors. In this connection, the Concessionaire shall, in                                        <br /><br /><br />
consultation with MIREM, propose and carry out an effective training and                                             <br /><br /><br />
employment programme for its Mozambican employees in each phase and level of                                         <br /><br /><br />
operations, taking account of the requirements of safety and the need to maintain                                    <br /><br /><br />
reasonable standards of efficiency in the conduct of the Petroleum Operations.                                       <br /><br /><br />
Such employees may be trained in the Republic of Mozambique or abroad as                                             <br /><br /><br />
required by the training programmes prepared by the Concessionaire.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
18.3    The Concessionaire shall co-operate with MIREM in giving a mutually agreed                                   <br /><br /><br />
number of Government employees the opportunity to participate in training                                            <br /><br /><br />
activities provided by the Concessionaire or any of its Affiliated Companies for its                                 <br /><br /><br />
employees and specifically for Government employees.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
18.4    In order for MIREM to monitor the fulfilment of the employment and training                                  <br /><br /><br />
obligations contained in this Article, the Concessionaire shall annually submit its                                  <br /><br /><br />
recruitment and training programmes to MIREM.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
18.5                         The Concessionaire shall pay one million United States dollars (US$ 1,000,000) to       <br /><br /><br />
                             the Government. This amount shall be used as institutional support to the entities      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                             involved in promotion and administration of Petroleum Operations. Such payment          <br /><br /><br />
                             shall be made within thirty (30) days from the Effective Date to the Government in      <br /><br /><br />
                             accordance with the instruction provided by the representative of the Government        <br /><br /><br />
(execution copy                                                          57                                          <br /><br /><br />
﻿ designated in this EPC.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
18.6    (a) During the Exploration Period, the Concessionaire shall pay to the               <br /><br /><br />
Government two hundred thousand United States Dollars (US$ 200,000)                          <br /><br /><br />
per year, to be spent on training and institutional support programmes                       <br /><br /><br />
within the Government. The Concessionaire and the Government may                             <br /><br /><br />
mutually agree to training activities to be funded by Concessionaire. In such                <br /><br /><br />
instances the agreed amount of funding shall be used as a credit against the                 <br /><br /><br />
following year’s training obligation. The first payment shall be made on the                 <br /><br /><br />
anniversary of the Effective Date within the Exploration Period of this EPC                  <br /><br /><br />
and subsequent payments shall be made on the anniversaries thereof.                          <br /><br /><br />
b) During the Development and Production Period the Concessionaire shall                     <br /><br /><br />
pay to the Government three hundred thousand United States Dollars                           <br /><br /><br />
(US$300,000) per year to be spent on training and institutional support                      <br /><br /><br />
programmes within the Government. The Concessionaire and the                                 <br /><br /><br />
Government may mutually agree to training activities to be funded by                         <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire. In such instances the agreed amount of funding shall be                      <br /><br /><br />
used as a credit against the following year’s training obligation. The first                 <br /><br /><br />
payment shall be made within thirty (30) days from the approval of the first                 <br /><br /><br />
Development Plan and subsequent payments shall be made on the                                <br /><br /><br />
anniversary thereof.                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
18.7    The Concessionaire shall pay to the Government two hundred and fifty thousand        <br /><br /><br />
United States dollars (US$ 250 000) for social support projects for the citizens of          <br /><br /><br />
the Republic of Mozambique in areas where Petroleum Operations take place. The               <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire may recommend social programs to be funded by the                             <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire and if agreed by the Government the agreed amount of funding                  <br /><br /><br />
shall be used as a credit against the following year social support obligation. The          <br /><br /><br />
first payment shall be made within thirty (30) days from the Effective Date. Such            <br /><br /><br />
annual amount to be paid by the Concessionaire until a total amount of one million           <br /><br /><br />
United States Dollars (USS 1.000.000) has been paid in full.                                 <br /><br /><br />
18.8    The Concessionaire shall include as part of the Development Plan proposals for the   <br /><br /><br />
activities required to satisfy the obligations contained in Article 18.3 during the          <br /><br /><br />
Execution cop}'    58                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
﻿ Development and Production Period.                                                      <br /><br /><br />

18.9 The sums expended by the Concessionaire to satisfy the obligations contained in     <br /><br /><br />
this article shall be recoverable costs for the purpose of Annex “C” of this EPC.        <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                       Article 19                              <br /><br /><br />
                                             Indemnification and Liability                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
19.1    The Concessionaire shall indemnify and hold the Government harmless from and           <br /><br /><br />
against any and all claims instituted against the Government by third parties in               <br /><br /><br />
respect of injury, loss or damage caused by the Concessionaire in the conduct of the           <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations in which the Concessionaire participates, provided that the               <br /><br /><br />
claims are duly qualified by a third party or the Government. In no case the                   <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire's liability under this Article shall include punitive damages.                  <br /><br /><br />
19.2    The Government shall indemnify and hold the Concessionaire, its Subcontractors         <br /><br /><br />
and any of its Affiliated Companies harmless from and against any and all claims               <br /><br /><br />
instituted against the Concessionaire, its Subcontractors and any of its Affiliated            <br /><br /><br />
Companies by third parties in respect of injury, loss or damage caused by the acts             <br /><br /><br />
or omissions of the Government in its commercial capacity.                                     <br /><br /><br />
19.3    Except as provided for in Article 19.8 no Party hereto shall settle or compromise      <br /><br /><br />
any claim for which another Party is responsible hereunder without the prior                   <br /><br /><br />
written consent of such other Party, and in the event that it does so, the indemnity           <br /><br /><br />
aforesaid shall not have effect in relation to the claim so settled or compromised.            <br /><br /><br />
19.4    Notwithstanding anything to the contrary in this EPC, the Concessionaire, its          <br /><br /><br />
Subcontractors and any of its Affiliated Companies carrying out such Petroleum                 <br /><br /><br />
Operations on behalf of the Concessionaire shall not be liable to the Government               <br /><br /><br />
and the Government shall not be liable to the Concessionaire, for consequential loss           <br /><br /><br />
or damage including but not limited to inability to produce Petroleum, loss of                 <br /><br /><br />
production, loss of profit or punitive damages.                                                <br /><br /><br />
 19.5    Subject to Article 19.4, in carrying out Petroleum Operations under this EPC the      <br /><br /><br />
 Concessionaire shall be liable for any injury, loss or damage suffered by the                 <br /><br /><br />
 Government and caused by the Concessionaire or by any Affiliated Company or                   <br /><br /><br />
 Subcontractor carrying out Petroleum Operations on behalf of the Concessionaire if            <br /><br /><br />
 such injury loss or damage is the result of the Concessionaire’s, the Affiliated              <br /><br /><br />
 Company’s or the Subcontractor’s failure to meet the standards required by this               <br /><br /><br />
 EPC.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
Invention copy    60                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿19.6    Any claim pursued by any third parties which would entitle any of the Parties            <br /><br /><br />
(together the ‘indemnified Party”) of this EPC to be indemnified by any of the                   <br /><br /><br />
other Parties of this EPC (together the “Indemnifying Party”) shall be promptly                  <br /><br /><br />
communicated by notice to the Parties so that the Indemnifying Party may promptly                <br /><br /><br />
intervene in the claim and pursue its defence. The Indemnified Party which is in                 <br /><br /><br />
breach of the obligation to notify the claim and causes the Indemnifying Party not               <br /><br /><br />
to be able to properly pursue its defence, shall loose its rights to the indemnification         <br /><br /><br />
under this Article.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
19.7    If within thirty (30) days of receipt of such claim notice, the Indemnifying Party       <br /><br /><br />
notifies the Indemnified Party that it elects to assume the defence of such claim,               <br /><br /><br />
then the Indemnifying Party shall have the rights to defend, at its cost and expense,            <br /><br /><br />
such claim by all appropriate proceedings including any compromise or settlement                 <br /><br /><br />
thereof, so long as any settlement agreement does not provide for or result in any               <br /><br /><br />
continuing liability or obligation on the Indemnified Party in respect of such third             <br /><br /><br />
party claim.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
19.8    If the Indemnifying Party fails timely to elect to assume the defence of such claim,     <br /><br /><br />
then the Indemnified Party shall have the right to defend at the sole cost and                   <br /><br /><br />
expense of the Indemnifying Party the third party claim by all appropriate                       <br /><br /><br />
proceedings including any compromise or settlement thereof.                                      <br /><br /><br />

﻿                               Article 20                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                    Title                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
20.1    Title to the Concessionaire’s entitlement of Petroleum Produced under this EPC           <br /><br /><br />
shall pass to the Concessionaire at the Wellhead. Thereafter the Government and                  <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire shall own the Petroleum jointly, and in undivided shares, until               <br /><br /><br />
each takes individual title to and delivery of its entitlement of Petroleum at the               <br /><br /><br />
Delivery Point.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
20.2    The Concessionaire shall finance the cost of all facilities and equipment to be used     <br /><br /><br />
in Petroleum Operations. Subject to applicable law and this Article the                          <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire shall have the right to use such equipment and facilities for                     <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire Petroleum Operations during the term of this EPC and any                          <br /><br /><br />
extensions thereof until the EPC expires, is surrendered or cancelled, in which case             <br /><br /><br />
the title to said facilities and equipment at the option of the Government and                   <br /><br /><br />
without additional compensation may be transferred to the Government. In the                     <br /><br /><br />
event that Government requires the transfer of such facilities and equipments to the             <br /><br /><br />
Government or to a Mozambican Person wholly owned or controlled by the                           <br /><br /><br />
Government, Concessionaire shall be released from all responsibility and liability               <br /><br /><br />
of every kind pertaining to decommissioning of such facilities and equipments as                 <br /><br /><br />
well as payment of any further funds in the Decommissioning Fund. Government                     <br /><br /><br />
shall indemnify Concessionaire from and against any loss, damage and liability of                <br /><br /><br />
any nature whatsoever, as well as any claim, action or proceeding instituted against             <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire by any person or entity, including, but not limited to any                        <br /><br /><br />
Governmental authority, arising from, or connected with, the continued use of such               <br /><br /><br />
facilities and equipments and their ultimate decommissioning, as well as any failure             <br /><br /><br />
by Government or person appointed by Government to properly decommissioning                      <br /><br /><br />
such facilities and equipments.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
20.3    The Concessionaire shall be the owner of facilities and necessary appurtenant            <br /><br /><br />
equipment for use in Petroleum Operations under this EPC unless otherwise                        <br /><br /><br />
approved by the Government. The provisions of Article 20.2 above with respect to                 <br /><br /><br />
the title of property passing to the Government shall not apply to equipment                     <br /><br /><br />
approved by the Government as belonging to third parties. Moveable facilities and                <br /><br /><br />
equipment owned by foreign third parties may be freely exported from the Republic                <br /><br /><br />
Kxscutfon copy    62                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
﻿of Mozambique in accordance with applicable law and the terms of the applicable              <br /><br /><br />
agreement.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
20.4    Third parties may subject to terms and conditions stipulated by applicable           <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum law have the right to the use available spare capacity of facilities and           <br /><br /><br />
necessary appurtenant equipment on terms and conditions to be agreed between the             <br /><br /><br />
parties and acceptable to the Government. Such terms and conditions shall include            <br /><br /><br />
a tariff that shall represent the payment for the Concessionaire's cost of additional        <br /><br /><br />
investments required for facilitating such third party use as well as operational costs      <br /><br /><br />
and a profit element reflecting the risk taken by the owner of the facilities. The           <br /><br /><br />
tariff for third party use of facilities and appurtenant equipment shall be approved         <br /><br /><br />
by the Government. When the Concessionaire and the third parties wishing to make             <br /><br /><br />
use of facilities can not agree to a reasonable tariff for third party use the               <br /><br /><br />
Government may stipulate the tariff.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
20.5    Third party use of facilities and necessary appurtenant equipment shall only take    <br /><br /><br />
place when such third party use is not materially negatively affecting                       <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire Petroleum Operations and is feasible from a technical,                        <br /><br /><br />
environmental and safety point of view.                                                      <br /><br /><br />

﻿                             Article 23                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                             Confidentiality                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
23.1    This EPC, the Documentation and other records, reports analyses, compilations,          <br /><br /><br />
data, studies and other materials (in whatever form maintained, whether                         <br /><br /><br />
documentary, computer storage or otherwise) are confidential (hereinafter referred              <br /><br /><br />
to as “Confidential Information”) and except as authorised by applicable law or this            <br /><br /><br />
Article shall not be disclosed to any third party without the prior written consent of          <br /><br /><br />
all the Parties hereto, which consent shall not be unreasonably withheld.                       <br /><br /><br />
23.2    Nothing in this Article shall prevent the disclosure of Documentation, excluding the    <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire’s interpretations and assessments, to a third party by the                       <br /><br /><br />
Government:                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    if it relates to an area which is no longer part of the EPC Area; or                    <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    with the written consent of the Concessionaire, which shall not be                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 unreasonably withheld if, in the judgment of the Government the                                <br /><br /><br />
 Documentation might have significance for the assessment of prospectivity                      <br /><br /><br />
 in an adjoining area over which the Government is offering Exploration                         <br /><br /><br />
 rights.                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
23.3 Restrictions on disclosure imposed by this Article shall not apply to a disclosure         <br /><br /><br />
made reasonably:                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    if it is required for the purpose of any arbitration or legal proceedings or            <br /><br /><br />
 claim relating to this EPC or to the Petroleum Operations;                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    to a Subcontractor, or consultant in connection with the conduct of                     <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum Operations;                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 (c) by the Concessionaire or Operator to a third party where such disclosure is                <br /><br /><br />
 essential to the safe conduct of Petroleum Operations;                                         <br /><br /><br />
﻿(e)    by the Concessionaire to a third party for the purpose of entering into a          <br /><br /><br />
contract for data exchange with another entity operating in Mozambique                    <br /><br /><br />
where all data exchanged relates to Petroleum Operations within                           <br /><br /><br />
Mozambique;                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(f)    by any Person constituting the Concessionaire to a bona fide intending             <br /><br /><br />
assignee of an interest under this EPC or an interest in any Person                       <br /><br /><br />
constituting the Concessionaire;                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(g)    to a third party in connection with and for the purpose of the sale or             <br /><br /><br />
proposed sale of Petroleum from the EPC Area;                                             <br /><br /><br />
(h)    to a third party in connection with the financing or proposed financing of         <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations;                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(i)    which is required by any applicable law or by the rules or regulations of any      <br /><br /><br />
recognised stock exchange on which shares of the disclosing Party or any of               <br /><br /><br />
its Affiliated Companies are listed; or                                                   <br /><br /><br />
(j)    if, and to the extent that, it is already public knowledge without improper        <br /><br /><br />
disclosure hereto.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
Any Confidential Information disclosed pursuant to paragraphs (b), (d), (e), (f) or       <br /><br /><br />
(h) of this Article 23.3 shall be disclosed on terms that ensure that such                <br /><br /><br />
Confidential Information is treated as confidential by the recipient.                     <br /><br /><br />
23.4 None of the Persons constituting the Concessionaire shall be required to disclose    <br /><br /><br />
any of its proprietary technology or that of their Affiliated Companies or                <br /><br /><br />
proprietary technology of a third party licensed to the Persons constituting the          <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire or the Operator.                                                           <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                 Article 24                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                 Assignment                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
24.1    Subject to Article 9.14 and this Article the Concessionaire, and where the                    <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire is more than one Person every Person who constitutes the                               <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire, may assign to another Person its rights and obligations hereunder                     <br /><br /><br />
or an undivided proportionate part thereof. The same applies to other direct and                      <br /><br /><br />
indirect transfers of interest or participation in the EPC, including, inter alia,                    <br /><br /><br />
assignment of shareholdings or any legal instrument which provides or may                             <br /><br /><br />
provide decisive control over a Person constituting the Concessionaire or its                         <br /><br /><br />
Participating Interest in this EPC. Save as provided in Article 24.2, an assignment                   <br /><br /><br />
shall require the prior written consent of the Minister of Mineral Resources.                         <br /><br /><br />
24.2    No consent shall be required by the Minister of Mineral Resources in case of an               <br /><br /><br />
assignor who is not in material breach of any of the terms and conditions hereof in                   <br /><br /><br />
respect of an assignment:                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(a)    as a result of an Assignment Notice served on a Defaulting Participant                         <br /><br /><br />
under this EPC; or                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(b)    if required to give effect to the default procedures under a joint operating                   <br /><br /><br />
agreement concluded in relation to the Petroleum Operations.                                          <br /><br /><br />
24.3    Each assignment made pursuant to this Article shall be effected by an instrument in           <br /><br /><br />
writing to be executed by the assignee on terms whereby such assignee accepts and                     <br /><br /><br />
agrees to become a Person constituting the Concessionaire and to be bound by the                      <br /><br /><br />
terms and conditions of this EPC including all appurtenant documents required by                      <br /><br /><br />
an administrative decision or applicable law and free of any transfer charge or fees.                 <br /><br /><br />
24.4    No unitisation pursuant to this EPC or applicable law or any adjustment to the                <br /><br /><br />
portion of the unitised Discovery allocated to the EPC Area shall be considered to                    <br /><br /><br />
be an assignment under this Article.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                           Article 25                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                          Force Majeure                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
25.1    The non-performance or delay in performance, wholly or in part, by the              <br /><br /><br />
Government or the Concessionaire of any obligation under this EPC excepting an              <br /><br /><br />
obligation to make payments hereunder, shall be excused if, and to the extent that,         <br /><br /><br />
such non-performance or delay is caused by Force Majeure.                                   <br /><br /><br />
25.2    For the purpose of this EPC, the term Force Majeure means any cause or event        <br /><br /><br />
beyond the reasonable control of, and not brought about at the instance of, the Party       <br /><br /><br />
claiming to be affected by such event, and which has caused the non-performance             <br /><br /><br />
or delay in performance. Without limitation to the generality of the foregoing,             <br /><br /><br />
events of Force Majeure shall include natural phenomena or calamities including             <br /><br /><br />
but not limited to, epidemics, earthquakes, storms, lightning, floods, fires,               <br /><br /><br />
blowouts, wars declared or undeclared, transboundary hostilities, blockades, civil          <br /><br /><br />
unrest or disturbances, labour disturbances, strikes, quarantine restrictions and           <br /><br /><br />
unlawful acts of government.                                                                <br /><br /><br />
25.3    The Party claiming suspension of its obligations under this EPC on account of       <br /><br /><br />
Force Majeure shall:                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(a)    promptly notify the other Parties of the occurrence thereof;                         <br /><br /><br />
(b)    take all actions that are reasonable and legal actions to remove the cause of        <br /><br /><br />
Force Majeure but nothing herein shall require the Concessionaire, subject                  <br /><br /><br />
to applicable law, to resolve any labour dispute except on terms satisfactory               <br /><br /><br />
to the Concessionaire; and                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
(c)    upon removal or termination thereof, promptly notify the other Parties and           <br /><br /><br />
take all reasonable action for the resumption of the performance of its                     <br /><br /><br />
obligations under this EPC as soon as possible after the removal or                         <br /><br /><br />
termination of Force Majeure.                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
 Kvi'Ctitioii copy                                          69                              <br /><br /><br />
﻿25.4    Where under this EPC the Concessionaire is required or has the right to do any act     <br /><br /><br />
or to carry out any programme within a specified period or the rights of the                   <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire hereunder are to subsist for a specified period the specified period            <br /><br /><br />
shall be extended so as to take reasonable account of any period during which by               <br /><br /><br />
reason of Force Majeure the Concessionaire has been unable to carry out the                    <br /><br /><br />
programme necessary to exercise a right, carry out its obligations or enjoy its rights         <br /><br /><br />
hereunder.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
25.5    Where a Force Majeure situation continues for more than fifteen (15) consecutive       <br /><br /><br />
days, the Parties shall meet forthwith in order to review the situation and to agree           <br /><br /><br />
on the measures to be taken for the removal of the cause of Force Majeure and for              <br /><br /><br />
the resumption in accordance with the provisions of this EPC of the performance                <br /><br /><br />
of the obligations hereunder.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
