﻿                                                             Article 26                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                      Foreign Exchange Control                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
26.1    The Concessionaire shall at all times comply with the procedures and formalities                                       <br /><br /><br />
relating to dealings in foreign exchange which may be in force in the Republic of                                              <br /><br /><br />
Mozambique from time to time and the Government undertakes to ensure that those                                                <br /><br /><br />
procedures and formalities will not in any way diminish the rights accorded to the                                             <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire under clauses 26.2 to 26.8.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
26.2    The Concessionaire shall have the right but not the obligation:                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(a)    to open and keep one or more accounts denominated in Mozambican                                                         <br /><br /><br />
currency with any bank in the Republic of Mozambique authorised by                                                             <br /><br /><br />
Banco de Mozambique for this purpose and to dispose freely of the sums                                                         <br /><br /><br />
deposited therein without restriction.                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Such accounts may be credited only with:                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(i)    the proceeds of the conversion into Mozambican currency pursuant                                                        <br /><br /><br />
to Article 26.2(c) of United States dollar funds deposited in the                                                              <br /><br /><br />
accounts referred to in Article 26.2(b);                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(ii)    the unused balance of any sums drawn from such account; and                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                         (iii)    amounts received in Mozambican currency in respect of funds                  <br /><br /><br />
                                         related to Petroleum Operations including sale of Petroleum or of                     <br /><br /><br />
                                         any rental, refund or other credit received by the Concessionaire                     <br /><br /><br />
                                         which apply to any charge made to the accounts under this EPC.                        <br /><br /><br />
(b)    to open and keep one or more accounts denominated in United States                                                      <br /><br /><br />
dollars, with any bank in the Republic of Mozambique authorised by Banco                                                       <br /><br /><br />
de Mozambique for this purpose, to freely import and deposit into such                                                         <br /><br /><br />
account funds required for the conduct of Petroleum Operations and to                                                          <br /><br /><br />
freely dispose of the sums deposited therein without restriction, provided                                                     <br /><br /><br />
always that such accounts are credited only with sums deposited in United                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 I'.W'Ciilion copy                                             71                                 JA                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                        States dollars;                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(c) to purchase Mozambican currency from banks in the Republic of                            <br /><br /><br />
Mozambique, exchange houses, other financial institutions, authorised by                     <br /><br /><br />
Banco de Mozambique for this purpose.                                                        <br /><br /><br />
26.3    (a) The Concessionaire and the Operator acting on behalf of the Concessionaire       <br /><br /><br />
shall have the right to open and keep up to four (4) accounts (as well to                    <br /><br /><br />
open and keep further accounts outside the Republic of Mozambique with                       <br /><br /><br />
the prior consent of the Bank of Mozambique) with any bank outside the                       <br /><br /><br />
Republic of Mozambique, in any foreign currency, and freely dispose of the                   <br /><br /><br />
sums deposited therein without restriction, with funds related to Petroleum                  <br /><br /><br />
Operations. Such accounts, however, shall not be credited with the proceeds                  <br /><br /><br />
of the sale of Mozambican currency without the prior consent of the Bank                     <br /><br /><br />
of Mozambique except for funds generated by the sale within the Republic                     <br /><br /><br />
of Mozambique of Petroleum, or of assets held in respect of Petroleum                        <br /><br /><br />
Operations, which may be credited to the aforesaid accounts without the                      <br /><br /><br />
need for prior consent.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Save in respect of funds needed by the Concessionaire to discharge its                <br /><br /><br />
obligations under this EPC to the Government, which payments may be                          <br /><br /><br />
made out of proceeds deposited in such offshore accounts, the                                <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire shall have the right to retain abroad all proceeds and                        <br /><br /><br />
payments under this EPC received in said bank accounts, and to dispose                       <br /><br /><br />
freely of the same without any obligation to convert the whole or any part of                <br /><br /><br />
such proceeds and payments to Mozambican currency or to otherwise                            <br /><br /><br />
repatriate the same or any part thereof to the Republic of Mozambique;                       <br /><br /><br />
provided, however, that subject to applicable law, the estimated amount of                   <br /><br /><br />
tax due in respect of the Concesssionare’s share of Profit Petroleum shall be                <br /><br /><br />
remitted to an account in the Republic of Mozambique within 45 days, and                     <br /><br /><br />
all amounts to which the Government is entitled shall be remitted to the                     <br /><br /><br />
Republic of Mozambique within 30 days.                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(c)    All payments to the Government and/or to ENH shall be made in United                  <br /><br /><br />
States dollars , unless the Parties have agreed otherwise, to two accounts                   <br /><br /><br />
 Execution copy                                                          72                  <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                  domiciled in the Republic of Mozambique, the first to be indicated by the                  <br /><br /><br />
                                  Government and the other by ENH.                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(d) The Concessionaire shall be obliged to report periodically on the operation                                              <br /><br /><br />
of the accounts referred to in clause 26.3(a), above. Specifically, the                                                      <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire shall copy the Government on monthly bank statements                                                          <br /><br /><br />
received. The Government shall be entitled to audit such accounts.                                                           <br /><br /><br />
Amounts spent on any such audits shall be cost recoverable. The                                                              <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire shall wave banking confidentiality as to the Government in                                                    <br /><br /><br />
respect of such accounts in order to facilitate any such audits.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
26.4    Subject to withholding tax due, all non-resident Subcontractor and all of the                                        <br /><br /><br />
Expatriate Personnel of the Concessionaire, the Operator or of any Subcontractors,                                           <br /><br /><br />
shall be entitled to receive in any currency other than Mozambican currency the                                              <br /><br /><br />
whole or any part of his compensation outside the Republic of Mozambique. All                                                <br /><br /><br />
payments to resident subcontractors shall be made exclusively in Mozambique.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
26.5    This foreign exchange regime shall not apply to ENH or its legal successor, in the                                   <br /><br /><br />
event that same is a Mozambican Person, as a Person constituting Concessionaire                                              <br /><br /><br />
under this EPC, which shall be subject to the regime set forth in applicable law.                                            <br /><br /><br />
26.6    Subject to clause 26.3(b), above, the Concessionaire may receive, remit and retain                                   <br /><br /><br />
abroad and freely dispose of all or any part of the proceeds realised from the sale of                                       <br /><br /><br />
its share of Petroleum, including the portion of Crude Oil for the recovery of costs                                         <br /><br /><br />
and the Profit Petroleum to which it is entitled.                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
26.7    Subject to withholding tax due, the Concessionaire shall have the right freely to                                    <br /><br /><br />
declare and pay dividends to their shareholders and to remit the same abroad under                                           <br /><br /><br />
the terms of the applicable law.                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
26.8    The Government and the Concessionaire shall develop procedures under which                                           <br /><br /><br />
amounts demonstrably expended under this EPC that are cost recoverable, as well                                              <br /><br /><br />
as such further amounts demonstrably expended as may be classifiable as capital                                              <br /><br /><br />
expense under applicable law, shall be entitled to capital registration                                                      <br /><br /><br />
notwithstanding the account from which the corresponding expenses were made.                                                 <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                      Article 27                                            <br /><br /><br />
                 Nature and Extent of the Rights of the Concessionaire                      <br /><br /><br />
27.1    Subject to any right that the Government may have under the laws of Mozambique      <br /><br /><br />
for imperative reasons in the national interest to acquire Petroleum to which the           <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire holds title, and the right of the Government to collect Petroleum            <br /><br /><br />
Production Tax in kind pursuant to Article 11.6 (d) the Concessionaire may, by              <br /><br /><br />
export or otherwise, freely sell or otherwise dispose of its entitlement to Petroleum       <br /><br /><br />
as provided for in this EPC.                                                                <br /><br /><br />
27.2    The rights granted under this EPC to the Concessionaire and its Subcontractors      <br /><br /><br />
shall include the right of use and enjoyment of the land and maritime areas                 <br /><br /><br />
encompassed in the EPC Area, for the purpose of conducting Petroleum                        <br /><br /><br />
Operations. For that purpose Concessionaire and its Subcontractors may construct            <br /><br /><br />
and operate such works, facilities, platforms, structures and pipelines as may be           <br /><br /><br />
necessary. Such rights to be exercised by the Concessionaire provided, however,             <br /><br /><br />
that the lawful occupier of any land in the EPC Area shall retain any rights he may         <br /><br /><br />
have to graze stock upon or cultivate the surface of the land, except to the extent         <br /><br /><br />
that such grazing or cultivation interferes with Petroleum Operations in any such           <br /><br /><br />
area. Further, for the purpose of conducting Petroleum Operations, Concessionaire           <br /><br /><br />
and its Subcontractors may conduct and operate works, facilities, platforms,                <br /><br /><br />
structures and pipelines necessary in the EPC area. Such rights to be exercised by          <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire, provided, however, that such Persons shall retain rights they           <br /><br /><br />
may have to fishing or aquaculture, except to the extent such activities interfere          <br /><br /><br />
with Petroleum Operations in such area.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
27.3    The right of the Concessionaire to use the land, maritime area or sea bed shall     <br /><br /><br />
continue to apply to acreage initially included within the EPC Area but                     <br /><br /><br />
subsequently relinquished in accordance with the terms of this EPC where such               <br /><br /><br />
use is reasonably necessary for purposes of conducting Petroleum Operations in the          <br /><br /><br />
EPC Area then remaining under this EPC.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
27.4 For the purposes of carrying out Petroleum Operations, the Concessionaire and any      <br /><br /><br />
Subcontractors shall have at all times access to and from the EPC Area and to any           <br /><br /><br />
other area in the Republic of Mozambique where the Concessionaire has acquired              <br /><br /><br />
 execution copy                                       75                                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿                    or constructed facilities, subject to Articles 27.9(f) and (g).                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
27.5    The rights of the Concessionaire under Articles 27.2, 27.3, 27.4, 27.8, and 27.9              <br /><br /><br />
shall be exercised reasonably so as to affect as little as possible the interests of any              <br /><br /><br />
lawful occupier of land in the EPC Area.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
27.6    Where in the course of conducting Petroleum Operations in the EPC Area the                    <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire causes disturbance to the rights of the lawful occupier of any land                    <br /><br /><br />
or causes damage to his growing crops, trees, buildings, stock or works the                           <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire shall pay to the lawful occupier such compensation in respect of                       <br /><br /><br />
any such disturbance or damage as may be agreed by a settlement or as                                 <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire may be adjudged liable to pay by final, non-appealable order or                        <br /><br /><br />
judgement of a court or arbitral body under Mozambican jurisdiction.                                  <br /><br /><br />
27.7    Where in the course of conducting Petroleum Operations in the EPC Area the                    <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire causes disturbance to the rights of a Person having their fishing                      <br /><br /><br />
fields or grounds occupied, aquaculture activities limited, fishing or aquaculture                    <br /><br /><br />
equipment moved to less favourable locations from a maritime resource                                 <br /><br /><br />
management or commercial point of view, as well as having their equipment, catch                      <br /><br /><br />
or harvest polluted or damaged the Concessionaire shall pay to the Person affected                    <br /><br /><br />
such compensation in respect of any such demonstrable disturbance or damage as                        <br /><br /><br />
may be agreed by settlement or as Concessionaire may be adjudged liable to pay by-                    <br /><br /><br />
final, non-appealable order or judgement of a court of or arbitral body under                         <br /><br /><br />
Mozambican jurisdiction.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
27.8    Where the amount of any compensation to be paid pursuant to Articles 27.6 and                 <br /><br /><br />
27.7 is in dispute, the matter shall be referred for determination to a sole expert                   <br /><br /><br />
pursuant to Article 30.6 as though it were a matter in dispute between the Parties.                   <br /><br /><br />
27.9    For the purposes described in this Article the following rights are granted to the            <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire subject to and in accordance with the provisions of the work                           <br /><br /><br />
programme related thereto and applicable law:                                                         <br /><br /><br />
              (a) to drill for and have the free use of water and impound surface waters and to       <br /><br /><br />
                     establish systems for the supply of water for the Petroleum Operations and       <br /><br /><br />
 Execution copy                                      76                                               <br /><br /><br />
﻿                               for consumption by its employees and its Subcontractors;                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    with the consent of, and subject to such terms and conditions agreed with,                      <br /><br /><br />
 any Person having the right to dispose of such minerals, to carry away and                             <br /><br /><br />
 use for Petroleum Operations in Mozambique, materials such as gravel,                                  <br /><br /><br />
 sand, lime, gypsum, stone and clay; provided that if the Person having the                             <br /><br /><br />
 right to dispose of the same is the Government or an agency of                                         <br /><br /><br />
 Government; then Concessionaire shall have the use of such minerals for                                <br /><br /><br />
 the Petroleum Operations in accordance with applicable law;                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    to erect, set up, maintain and operate engines, machinery, pipelines,                           <br /><br /><br />
 gathering lines, umbilicals, storage tanks, compressor stations, pumping                               <br /><br /><br />
 stations, houses, buildings and all other constructions, installations, works,                         <br /><br /><br />
 platforms, facilities and other fixtures which are required in furtherance of                          <br /><br /><br />
 its Petroleum Operations;                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 (d)    to erect, set up, maintain and operate all communication and transportation                     <br /><br /><br />
 systems and facilities but shall not, save for temporary purposes, do so                               <br /><br /><br />
 unless drawings of and locations for their sites have been submitted to and                            <br /><br /><br />
 approved by the Government, under reasonable conditions of installation                                <br /><br /><br />
 and operation of such systems and facilities;                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 (e) to erect, maintain and operate harbour and terminal facilities for use                             <br /><br /><br />
 exclusively in Petroleum Operations, together with the necessary means of                              <br /><br /><br />
 communication and transport between such facilities and any part of the                                <br /><br /><br />
 EPC Area; provided that the consent of the Government to the location of                               <br /><br /><br />
 such works shall first be obtained;                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 (f) with respect to lands located outside of the EPC Area, to have the right of                        <br /><br /><br />
 way over land not in the beneficial occupation of any Person and in the case                           <br /><br /><br />
 of land in the beneficial occupation of the Government or any state                                    <br /><br /><br />
 company, agency or instrumentality of the Government to have right of way                              <br /><br /><br />
 on such reasonable terms and conditions as the Government and the                                      <br /><br /><br />
 Concessionaire may agree; and                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />

﻿(g) with respect to lands located outside of the EPC Area, to have, otherwise                 <br /><br /><br />
than aforesaid, the use of land necessarily required for the conduct of                       <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations with the agreement of the Person holding a right                         <br /><br /><br />
affected, including the lawful occupier of land or, in the case of unoccupied                 <br /><br /><br />
land or land occupied by the Government or any state company, agency or                       <br /><br /><br />
instrumentality of the Government on such reasonable terms and conditions                     <br /><br /><br />
as the Government shall specify, provided that if the Concessionaire is                       <br /><br /><br />
unable to reach agreement with the Person so affected on the terms and                        <br /><br /><br />
conditions for the use of any such right including land the Concessionaire                    <br /><br /><br />
shall immediately notify the Government. If the use of the rights by the                      <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire is to be of a temporary nature, not exceeding one (1) year,                    <br /><br /><br />
the Government shall authorise such temporary use upon deposit by the                         <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire with the Government of a sum by way of compensation to                         <br /><br /><br />
such Person holding the right for loss of use and damage to its interest. If                  <br /><br /><br />
the use is required to be for a period longer than one (1) year, the                          <br /><br /><br />
Government shall authorise the use by the Concessionaire of the right in                      <br /><br /><br />
question upon deposit by the Concessionaire with the Government of such                       <br /><br /><br />
sum by way of compensation and shall direct appropriate proceedings to                        <br /><br /><br />
grant the Concessionaire the right to use and legally utilize the right under                 <br /><br /><br />
the law at the moment in force as if the Petroleum Operations were in all                     <br /><br /><br />
respects a work of public utility.                                                            <br /><br /><br />
27.10    The Concessionaire shall be subject to the procedures and formalities required by    <br /><br /><br />
applicable law for the exercise of the rights set forth in this Article.                      <br /><br /><br />
27.11    (a) In the event that the Government exercises any right it may have under the       <br /><br /><br />
 applicable laws to acquire for imperative reasons in the national interest                   <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum belonging to the Concessionaire, the Government shall give not                     <br /><br /><br />
 less than forty five (45) days notice of the exercise of such right and of the               <br /><br /><br />
 volumes it wishes to acquire, and the Concessionaire shall supply the                        <br /><br /><br />
 volumes so notified from the Petroleum to which the Concessionaire is                        <br /><br /><br />
 entitled under this EPC at the Delivery Point or such point that may be                      <br /><br /><br />
 agreed or such point within Mozambican jurisdiction designated by the                        <br /><br /><br />
 Government. Additional cost incurred by Concessionaire in order to deliver                   <br /><br /><br />
 such Petroleum at any other point than the Delivery Point with facilities and                <br /><br /><br />

                                                                   f                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
﻿ equipment in place, as well as other necessary costs related to the delivery                                      <br /><br /><br />
 of such Petroleum, shall be reimbursed to the Concessionaire by                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 Government and the cost of any new facilities and equipment to be used for                                        <br /><br /><br />
 such delivery shall be paid by the Government.                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    The Government shall pay the Concessionaire the full market value of the                                   <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum so acquired determined in accordance with Article 10. Payment                                           <br /><br /><br />
 for the Petroleum so acquired in any calendar month shall be made in                                              <br /><br /><br />
 United States dollars within thirty (30) days after the end of that calendar                                      <br /><br /><br />
 month. The Concessionaire may receive, remit and retain abroad and freely                                         <br /><br /><br />
 dispose of all or any part of the sums so paid.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    The Government shall not exercise its right to acquire Petroleum belonging                                 <br /><br /><br />
 to the Concessionaire:                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 (i)    in respect of any month unless during that month the Government is                                         <br /><br /><br />
 taking Petroleum Production Tax entirely in kind pursuant to                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 Article 11.5;                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (ii)    unless it is also exercising the same right rateably among all                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 producers of Petroleum within the Republic of Mozambique (to the                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 extent practicable taking into account the geographical location of                                               <br /><br /><br />
 the production in relation to the geographical location of the                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 requirements).                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
27.12 The Government undertakes that so long as this EPC subsists:                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 (a) The Government, its political subdivisions, agencies and instrumentalities,                                   <br /><br /><br />
 to the extent that they have or may acquire the power to do so, will not                                          <br /><br /><br />
 expropriate, nationalise or intervene in the assets, rights, interests or any                                     <br /><br /><br />
 other property of any kind of the Concessionaire held for the purpose of                                          <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum Operations including the rights held by the Concessionaire                                              <br /><br /><br />
 hereunder.                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                       Without prejudice to the rights of the Government acting through MIREM      <br /><br /><br />
Execution copy-                                      79                                             V              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
﻿          to regulate Petroleum Operations in the Republic of Mozambique, for the         <br /><br /><br />
          purpose of this undertaking, the Government shall be deemed to have             <br /><br /><br />
          intervened in the property or assets of the Concessionaire if (otherwise than   <br /><br /><br />
          pursuant to a judgment or in exercise of its rights as a mortgage creditor, or  <br /><br /><br />
          in accordance with the law of insolvency, liquidation or creditor’s rights) it  <br /><br /><br />
          assumes power of management over such property or assets or exercises           <br /><br /><br />
          effective control of such property or assets.                                   <br /><br /><br />
      (b) In the event of a breach of Article 27.12(a), nothing in the provisions of      <br /><br /><br />
          Article 19.5 shall be read or construed as preventing consideration of the      <br /><br /><br />
          projected flow of profits (if any) from Petroleum Operations hereunder for      <br /><br /><br />
          the purpose of determining the value of property or assets expropriated,        <br /><br /><br />
          nationalised or made subject to intervention.                                   <br /><br /><br />
      (c) In the event that the Petroleum Law is repealed or amended, the                 <br /><br /><br />
          Government undertakes to ensure that this EPC remains in full force and         <br /><br /><br />
          effect provided always that nothing in this provision will be construed as      <br /><br /><br />
          requiring the Government to relieve the Concessionaire from compliance          <br /><br /><br />
          with the provisions of applicable law relating to Petroleum Operations, not     <br /><br /><br />
          inconsistent herewith, which may be in force from time to time.                 <br /><br /><br />
27.13 (a) Where for the purpose of conducting Petroleum Operations hereunder the          <br /><br /><br />
          Concessionaire, Operator or any Subcontractor requires from MIREM, the          <br /><br /><br />
          Government or from any agency or instrumentality of the Government or           <br /><br /><br />
          from a political subdivision thereof any approvals, licences, permits,          <br /><br /><br />
          authorisations, consents or releases or any assistance, advice or guidance      <br /><br /><br />
          relating to the above, then subject to the terms and conditions of this EPC,    <br /><br /><br />
          the same shall be granted or given expeditiously and without undue delay.       <br /><br /><br />
      (b) Without prejudice to the generality thereof, the undertaking set out in         <br /><br /><br />
          Article 27.13(a) shall apply to:                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
           formalities relating to the import and export of goods including the           <br /><br /><br />
           export of Petroleum Produced hereunder;                                        <br /><br /><br />
           formalities relating to the use by the Concessionaire of any form of           <br /><br /><br />
﻿transport for the movement of employees, equipment and materials                                        <br /><br /><br />
and to the use of communication and port facilities in the Republic                                     <br /><br /><br />
of Mozambique;                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

-    approval of assignments and, to the extent required, transactions                                  <br /><br /><br />
relating to the shares of any Person constituting the Concessionaire.                                   <br /><br /><br />

The Government will expedite all formalities regarding the                                              <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire’s registration to do business in Republic of Mozambique                                  <br /><br /><br />
and the registration of any leases, contracts or other documents. The                                   <br /><br /><br />

reasonable protection in Republic of Mozambique.                                                        <br /><br /><br />

affecting Petroleum Operations that may, individually or in the aggregate, create a                     <br /><br /><br />

above-mentioned situations occur, meet to verify and agree on the changes, in all                       <br /><br /><br />
cases, that may be required to the EPC in order to restore, as closely as possible, the                 <br /><br /><br />
economic benefits that the Concessionaire would have derived if the change in the                       <br /><br /><br />
legislation had not been effected.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                 Article 28                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                        Protection of the Environment                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
28.1    The Government will at all times during the life of the Petroleum Operations ensure      <br /><br /><br />
in accordance with this Article, that measures taken in the interest of safety, health,          <br /><br /><br />
welfare or the protection of the environment are in accordance with standards                    <br /><br /><br />
generally accepted from time to lime in the international petroleum industry and are             <br /><br /><br />
not unreasonable.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
28.2    In carrying out Petroleum Operations hereunder the Concessionaire shall:                 <br /><br /><br />
(a)    in accordance with accepted standards in the international petroleum                      <br /><br /><br />
industry employ up-to-date techniques, practices and methods of operation                        <br /><br /><br />
for the prevention of environmental damage, the control of waste and the                         <br /><br /><br />
avoidance of unnecessary loss of, or damage to, natural resources;                               <br /><br /><br />
(b)    observe applicable laws and regulations of general application in force from              <br /><br /><br />
time to time in the Republic of Mozambique for the protection of the                             <br /><br /><br />
environment; and                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(c)    comply strictly with the obligations relating to the protection of the                    <br /><br /><br />
environment it has assumed under any approved Development Plan .                                 <br /><br /><br />
28.3    The Concessionaire undertakes for the purposes of this EPC to take all necessary         <br /><br /><br />
and adequate steps in accordance with Good Oilfield Practice to:                                 <br /><br /><br />
(a)    ensure, if the Concessionaire is otherwise legally responsible, proper                    <br /><br /><br />
compensation for injury to Persons or damage to property caused by the                           <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations;                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(b)    avoid irremediable environmental damage to the EPC Area and adjoining or                  <br /><br /><br />
neighbouring lands and marine areas caused by the Concessionaire’s                               <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations; and                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(c)    rehabilitate at its own cost all areas that suffer environmental damage as a              <br /><br /><br />
Execution copy                                 83                                                <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                 result of the Petroleum Operations.                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
28.4 If the Concessionaire fails to comply with the terms of Articles 28.2 or 28.3 or      <br /><br /><br />
contravenes any law on the prevention of environmental damage and such failure or          <br /><br /><br />
contravention results in any environmental damage, the Concessionaire shall take           <br /><br /><br />
all necessary and reasonable measures to remedy such failure or contravention and          <br /><br /><br />
the effects thereof.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
28.5    (a) If the Government has reasonable grounds to believe that any works or          <br /><br /><br />
installations erected by the Concessionaire or any operations carried out by               <br /><br /><br />
the Concessionaire in the EPC Area are endangering or may endanger                         <br /><br /><br />
Persons or any property of any other Person or is causing pollution or                     <br /><br /><br />
harming wildlife or the environment to a degree which the Government                       <br /><br /><br />
considers unacceptable, the Government shall notify the Concessionaire of                  <br /><br /><br />
its concerns and the Government and the Concessionaire shall immediately                   <br /><br /><br />
consult to agree on remedial measures to be taken by the Concessionaire.                   <br /><br /><br />
Said remedial measures will be undertaken w'ithin a reasonable period of                   <br /><br /><br />
time to repair any damage and to prevent further damage to the extent                      <br /><br /><br />
reasonably practicable. If there is a disagreement between the Government                  <br /><br /><br />
and the Concessionaire regarding the existence of a problem of the type                    <br /><br /><br />
described in this Article or the remedial action to be taken by the                        <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire, such matter shall be submitted to a sole expert for                        <br /><br /><br />
determination pursuant to Article 30.6.                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(b) in the case of any matter referred to a sole expert under Article 28.5(a), if          <br /><br /><br />
requested by the Government, the Concessionaire shall undertake such                       <br /><br /><br />
temporary measures to address the Government’s concerns as may be                          <br /><br /><br />
reasonably requested by the Government.                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
28.6 Without limitation to the generality of Articles 28.2, 28.3, 28.4 and 28.5, the       <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire shall cause a consulting firm or individuals, approved by the               <br /><br /><br />
Government on account of their special knowledge of environmental matters, to              <br /><br /><br />
carry out an environmental impact study on terms of reference determined by the            <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire and approved by the Government, in order to establish what the              <br /><br /><br />
effect will be on the environment, human beings, wildlife or marine life in the EPC        <br /><br /><br />
l.U'ciitliin copy                              84                                          <br /><br /><br />
﻿ Area in consequence of the Petroleum Operations to be undertaken under this EPC                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
28.7    If the Concessionaire fails to comply with any terms contained in this Article               <br /><br /><br />
within a reasonable period of time the Government may, after giving the                              <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire notice of such failure to comply and a reasonable period of time                      <br /><br /><br />
necessary to take corrective action, take any action which may be necessary to cure                  <br /><br /><br />
such failure, and recover, immediately after having taken such action, all                           <br /><br /><br />
expenditure incurred in connection with such action from the Concessionaire                          <br /><br /><br />
together with interest at the prevailing LIBOR rate calculated from the date such                    <br /><br /><br />
expenditure is made until repaid. “LIBOR” meaning the annual rate equal to the                       <br /><br /><br />
average three (3) month term compounded quarterly at the London inter-bank                           <br /><br /><br />
offered rate for United States dollar deposits as published by the Wall Street                       <br /><br /><br />
Journal or, if not published therein, then by the Financial Times of London. Should                  <br /><br /><br />
a rate not be quoted for a relevant date (such as weekends or public holidays), then                 <br /><br /><br />
the first subsequent quoted rate shall be used.                                                      <br /><br /><br />

archaeologically, historically or similarly protected areas or features which might                  <br /><br /><br />
be affected by the Petroleum Operations.                                                             <br /><br /><br />

boundaries of any protected area within the EPC Area, the Concessionaire shall                       <br /><br /><br />
obtain such additional approvals from the Government, as may be required by                          <br /><br /><br />
applicable law.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />

(i)    no surrender by the Concessionaire of its rights over any part of the                                                <br /><br /><br />

as set out in Article 4; and                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(ii)    any area surrendered shall be continuously delineated by meridians                                                  <br /><br /><br />
and parallels of latitude expressed in whole minutes of a degree.                                                           <br /><br /><br />

which accrued prior to the assignment.                                                    <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                                                 Article 30                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                              Consultation, Arbitration and Independent Expert                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
30.1    For the purpose of this article there are two Parties, the Government and the                                          <br /><br /><br />
Concessionaire.                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
30.2    A dispute shall be resolved, if possible, by negotiation between the Parties. A                                        <br /><br /><br />
notice of the existence of a dispute shall be given by a Party to another in                                                   <br /><br /><br />
accordance with the provisions of Article 35. In the event that no agreement is                                                <br /><br /><br />
reached within thirty (30) days after the date one Party notifies the other that a                                             <br /><br /><br />
dispute exists, or such longer period that is specifically provided for elsewhere in                                           <br /><br /><br />
this EPC, either Party shall have the right to have such dispute determined by-                                                <br /><br /><br />
arbitration or an expert as provided for in this Article 30. Arbitration and expert                                            <br /><br /><br />
determination as aforesaid shall be the exclusive method of determining a dispute                                              <br /><br /><br />
under this EPC.                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 30.3 Subject to the provisions of this Article 30, and save for any matter to be referred to                                  <br /><br /><br />
 a sole expert as provided in clause 30.6, the Parties shall submit any dispute arising                                        <br /><br /><br />
 out of or in connection with this EPC which cannot be resolved by negotiation as                                              <br /><br /><br />
 provided in clause 30.2 to arbitration as hereinafter provided:                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 (a) the dispute shall be submitted to the International Centre for Settlement of                                              <br /><br /><br />
 Investment Disputes (“ICSID”) for settlement by arbitration pursuant to the                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 Convention on the Settlement of Investment Disputes between States and                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 Nationals of Other States in accordance with the arbitration rules thereof in                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 effect on the Effective Date (the “Convention”). It is hereby stipulated that                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 the transaction to which this EPC relates is an investment;                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                 (b) the seat of the arbitration shall be Geneva, Switzerland and the law of the               <br /><br /><br />
                                 merits of the arbitration shall be Mozambique law. The arbitration shall be                   <br /><br /><br />
                                 conducted in the English language. If for any reason an ICSID arbitral                        <br /><br /><br />
                                 tribunal declines to approve Geneva as the place of arbitration, the place of                 <br /><br /><br />
                                 arbitration for that case shall be the Permanent Court of Arbitration in the                  <br /><br /><br />
                                 Hague. Notwithstanding Article 32, the English version of this EPC signed                     <br /><br /><br />
                                 by the Parties shall be used as the official translation in arbitral proceedings;             <br /><br /><br />

                 t.u'ctitfon copy                                           91                                                 <br /><br /><br />

 arbitration or an arbitral tribunal established in accordance with the ICSID            <br /><br /><br />
 Arbitration Rules determines that the dispute is not within the jurisdiction of         <br /><br /><br />
 the Centre, the dispute shall be settled by arbitration in accordance with the          <br /><br /><br />

 between them subject to acceptance by the nominated arbitrator; provided                <br /><br /><br />

proceedings pursuant to this Article 30 shall be binding on the Parties and judgment                           <br /><br /><br />

or decision including, without limitation, immunity from service of process                                    <br /><br /><br />

the Concessionaire.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
30.5    Any matter in dispute of a technical nature not involving interpretation of law or                     <br /><br /><br />
the application of this EPC and which is required to be referred to a sole expert for                          <br /><br /><br />
determination under the provisions of this EPC, including Articles 10.3 (e) and 28.5                           <br /><br /><br />

Parties may otherwise agree to so refer) shall be referred by a Party giving notice to                         <br /><br /><br />
such effect pursuant to Article 35. Such notice shall contain a statement describing                           <br /><br /><br />
the dispute and all relevant information associated therewith. A sole expert shall be                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 Execution copy                                                  93                                            <br /><br /><br />
﻿an independent and impartial person of international standing with relevant                                               <br /><br /><br />
qualifications and experience appointed pursuant to the mutual agreement of the                                           <br /><br /><br />
Parties. Any sole expert appointed shall act as an expert and not as an arbitrator or                                     <br /><br /><br />
mediator and shall be instructed to endeavour to resolve the dispute referred to him                                      <br /><br /><br />
within thirty (30) days of his appointment, but in any event within sixty (60) days                                       <br /><br /><br />
of the appointment. Upon the selection of the sole expert, the Party receiving the                                        <br /><br /><br />
notice of referral above shall submit its own statement containing all information it                                     <br /><br /><br />
considers relevant with respect to the matter in dispute. The decision of the sole                                        <br /><br /><br />
expert shall be final and binding and not subject to any appeal, save for fraud,                                          <br /><br /><br />
corruption or manifest disregard of applicable procedure of this EPC. If the Parties                                      <br /><br /><br />
are unable to agree on the appointment of a sole expert within twenty (20) days                                           <br /><br /><br />
after a Party has received a notice of referral under this Article the sole expert shall                                  <br /><br /><br />
be selected by the ICC Centre for Expertise, and the person so selected shall be                                          <br /><br /><br />
appointed by the Parties.                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
30.6 The sole expert shall decide the maimer in which any determination is made,                                          <br /><br /><br />
including whether the Parties shall make oral or written submissions and                                                  <br /><br /><br />
arguments, and the Parties shall co-operate with the sole expert and provide such                                         <br /><br /><br />
documentation and information as the sole expert may request. All correspondence,                                         <br /><br /><br />
documentation and information provided by a Party to the sole expert shall be                                             <br /><br /><br />
copied to the other Party, and any oral submissions to the sole expert shall be made                                      <br /><br /><br />
in the presence of all Parties and each Party shall have a right of response. The sole                                    <br /><br /><br />
expert may obtain any independent professional or technical advice as the sole                                            <br /><br /><br />
expert considers necessary. The English version of this EPC signed by the Parties                                         <br /><br /><br />
shall be used as the official translation in any determination by the sole expert. The                                    <br /><br /><br />
fees and expenses of a sole expert appointed under the provisions of Article 30.5                                         <br /><br /><br />
shall be borne equally by the Parties.                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                       Article 31                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                       Applicable Law                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
31.1        This EPC shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the applicable            <br /><br /><br />
            laws of the Republic of Mozambique.                                                      <br /><br /><br />
            (a)    The Government and the Concessionaire agree to cooperate on preventing            <br /><br /><br />
31.2                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
            corruption. The parties undertake to take administrative disciplinary actions            <br /><br /><br />
            and rapid legal measures in their respective responsibilities to stop,                   <br /><br /><br />
            investigate and prosecute in accordance with national law any person                     <br /><br /><br />
            suspected of corruption or other intentional misuse resource.                            <br /><br /><br />
            (b)    No offer, gift, payments or benefit of any kind, which would or could be          <br /><br /><br />
            construed as an illegal or corrupt practice, shall be accepted, either directly          <br /><br /><br />
            or indirectly, as an inducement or reward for the execution of this EPC or               <br /><br /><br />
            for doing or not doing any action or making any decision in relation to this             <br /><br /><br />
            EPC.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
            (c)    The above is equally applicable to the Concessionaire, its Affiliated             <br /><br /><br />
            Companies, agents, representatives, sub-contractors or consultants when                  <br /><br /><br />
            such offer, gift, payments or benefit violate:                                           <br /><br /><br />
            (i)    the applicable laws of the Republic of Mozambique;                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
            (ii)    the laws of the country of formation of the Concessionaire or of its             <br /><br /><br />
            ultimate parent company (or its principal place of business); or,                        <br /><br /><br />
            (iii)    the principles described in the Convention on Combating Bribeiy of              <br /><br /><br />
            Foreign Public Officials in International Business Transactions,                         <br /><br /><br />
            signed in Paris on December 17, 1997, which entered into force on                        <br /><br /><br />
            February 15, 1999, and the Convention's Commentaries.                                    <br /><br /><br />
            References in this EPC to applicable law are without prejudice to the rights of the      <br /><br /><br />
31.3                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
            Parties under Article 27.14 when such applicable law is Mozambican law.                  <br /><br /><br />

﻿Annex C EPC Accounting and Financial Procedure                                                       <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                            Production Concession Contract dated December , 2006, awarded by         <br /><br /><br />
                            the Government of the Republic of Mozambique to Eni East Africa S.p.A    <br /><br /><br />
                            and Empresa Nacional de Hidrocarbonetos, (ENH) E.P (hereinafter          <br /><br /><br />
                            referred to as "the EPC").                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />

﻿Section 1 General Provisions                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
1.1 Definitions                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
For the purposes of this EPC Accounting and Financial Procedure the                  <br /><br /><br />
terms used here in which are defined in applicable law, the EPC shall                <br /><br /><br />
have the same meaning when used in this EPC Accounting and Financial                 <br /><br /><br />
Procedure.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
1.2 Statements required to be submitted by the Concessionaire                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    Within ninety (90) days of the Effective Date, the Concessionaire shall      <br /><br /><br />
 submit to the Government a proposed outline of charts of accounts,                  <br /><br /><br />
 operating records and reports, which outline shall be in accordance with            <br /><br /><br />
 applicable Mozambican law and generally accepted and recognised                     <br /><br /><br />
 accounting principles, consistent with best practice in the international           <br /><br /><br />
 petroleum industry. Within ninety (90) days of receiving the above                  <br /><br /><br />
 submission Government shall either indicate its approval of the proposal            <br /><br /><br />
 or request revisions to the proposal. Within one hundred and eighty (180)           <br /><br /><br />
 days after the Government has approved the Concessionaire’s proposals,              <br /><br /><br />
 the Concessionaire and Government shall approve an outline charts of                <br /><br /><br />
 accounts, operating records and reports which shall describe the basis of           <br /><br /><br />
 the accounting system and procedures to be developed and used under                 <br /><br /><br />
 the EPC. Following such approval, the Concessionaire shall expeditiously            <br /><br /><br />
 prepare and provide the Government with formal copies of the                        <br /><br /><br />
 comprehensive charts of accounts related to the accounting, recording               <br /><br /><br />
 and reporting functions, and allow Government to examine the                        <br /><br /><br />
 Concessionaire's manuals, if any, and to review procedures which are,               <br /><br /><br />
 and shall be, observed under the EPC.                                               <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    Notwithstanding the generality of the foregoing, the Concessionaire is       <br /><br /><br />
 required to make regular statements relating to the Petroleum Operations.           <br /><br /><br />
 These Statements are as follows:                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (i)    Production Statement (see Section 5 of this Annex);                          <br /><br /><br />
 (ii)    Value of Production and Petroleum Production Tax Statement (see             <br /><br /><br />
 Section 6 of this Annex);                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (iii)    Cost Recovery Statement (see Section 7 of this Annex);                     <br /><br /><br />
 (iv)    Statement of Expenditures and Receipts (see Section 8 of this               <br /><br /><br />
 Annex);                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (v)    Final End-of-Year Statement (see Section 9 of this Annex);                   <br /><br /><br />
 (vi)    Budget Statement (see Section 10 of this Annex);                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (vii)    Long Range Plans (see Section 11 of this Annex).                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (c) All reports and statements will be prepared in accordance with the EPC,         <br /><br /><br />
 applicable law and, where there are no relevant provisions in either of             <br /><br /><br />
 these, in accordance with generally accepted and recognised accounting              <br /><br /><br />
 principles consistent with best practice in the international petroleum             <br /><br /><br />
 industry.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
I'.xccutlon itup)                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                       Page 5 of 28                  <br /><br /><br />
﻿1.3 Language and Units of Account                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    Accounts shall be maintained in United States dollars and such          <br /><br /><br />
 other currency as may be required under the applicable law. United             <br /><br /><br />
 States dollars shall be the currency of reference for cost recovery            <br /><br /><br />
 purposes. Metric units and barrels shall be employed for measurements          <br /><br /><br />
 required under this Annex. The language employed shall be English and          <br /><br /><br />
 such other language as may be required under the applicable law. Where         <br /><br /><br />
 necessary for clarification the Concessionaire may also maintain accounts      <br /><br /><br />
 and records in other languages, units of measurement and currencies.           <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    It is the intent of this Accounting and Financial Procedure that        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 neither Government nor the Concessionaire should experience an                 <br /><br /><br />
 exchange gain or loss at the expense of, or to the benefit of, the other.      <br /><br /><br />
 However, should there be any gain or loss from exchange of currency, it        <br /><br /><br />
 will be credited or charged to the accounts under the EPC.                     <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    Amounts received and costs and expenditures made in                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 Mozambican Meticais or in United States dollars shall be converted from        <br /><br /><br />
 Mozambican Meticais into United States dollars or from United States           <br /><br /><br />
 dollars into Mozambican Meticais on the basis of the average of the            <br /><br /><br />
 buying and selling exchange rates between the currencies in question as        <br /><br /><br />
 published by Banco de Mocambique or in accordance with the applicable          <br /><br /><br />
 law, prevailing on the actual day of the transaction on which such             <br /><br /><br />
 amounts are received and costs and expenditures are paid or as agreed          <br /><br /><br />
 by the Parties.;                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
1.4 Payments                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Except as provided in Subsections 1.4(b) and (c), all payments between   <br /><br /><br />
the Parties shall, unless otherwise agreed, be in United States dollars and     <br /><br /><br />
through a bank designated by each receiving party.                              <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Payment of any tax by the Concessionaire shall be made in accordance     <br /><br /><br />
with the provisions of the EPC and the applicable law.                          <br /><br /><br />
(c)    Discharge of the Concessionaire's obligation with respect to the         <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Production Tax and the Government's share of Profit                   <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum shall be made in accordance with the EPC.                             <br /><br /><br />
(d)    All sums due by a Concessionaire to the Government under the EPC         <br /><br /><br />
during any calendar month shall, for each day such sums are overdue             <br /><br /><br />
during such month, bear interest compounded quarterly at an annual rate         <br /><br /><br />
equal to the average three (3) month London interbank offered rate              <br /><br /><br />
(LIBOR) plus one (1) percentage points for United States dollar deposits        <br /><br /><br />
as published by the Wall Street Journal or, rf not published therein, then      <br /><br /><br />
by the Financial Times of London. Should a rate not be quoted for a             <br /><br /><br />
relevant date (such as weekends or public holidays), then the first             <br /><br /><br />
subsequent quoted rate shall be used.                                           <br /><br /><br />
﻿1.5. Audit and Inspection Rights of the Government                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    Upon giving the Concessionaire thirty (30) days notice, the competent        <br /><br /><br />
 authority of the Government shall have the right to audit the                       <br /><br /><br />
 Concessionaire's accounts and records maintained in accordance with the             <br /><br /><br />
 EPC provisions with respect to each calendar year within three (3) years            <br /><br /><br />
 from the end of each such calendar year. An audit report with respect to            <br /><br /><br />
 Concessionaire’s accounts of any calendar year must be submitted to the             <br /><br /><br />
 Concessionaire within three (3) years from the end of such calendar year.           <br /><br /><br />
 For purposes of auditing, the Government may examine and verify at                  <br /><br /><br />
 reasonable times all charges and credits relating to the Petroleum                  <br /><br /><br />
 Operations such as books of account, accounting entries, material                   <br /><br /><br />
 records and any other documents, correspondence and records                         <br /><br /><br />
 necessary to audit and verify the charges and credits. Furthermore the              <br /><br /><br />
 auditors shall have the right in connection with such audit to visit and            <br /><br /><br />
 inspect, subject to reasonable notification, all sites, plants, facilities,         <br /><br /><br />
 warehouses and offices of the Concessionaire serving the Petroleum                  <br /><br /><br />
 Operations including visiting personnel associated with those operations.           <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    Without prejudice to the finality of matters as described in Subsection      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 1.5(a) all documents referred to in that sub-section shall be maintained            <br /><br /><br />
 and made available for inspection by the Government for such a time as              <br /><br /><br />
 prescribed by the applicable law.                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    In the event that Government does not conduct an audit with respect to a     <br /><br /><br />
 calendar year or conducts the audit but does not issue an audit report              <br /><br /><br />
 within the time specified in Subsection 1.5 (a) above , Government shall            <br /><br /><br />
 be deemed not to have objected the Cost Recovery Statement prepared                 <br /><br /><br />
 and maintained by the Concessionaire and such Cost Recovery                         <br /><br /><br />
 Statement shall be considered true and correct for Cost Recovery                    <br /><br /><br />
 purposes for such calendar year absent material mistake, fraud or willful           <br /><br /><br />
 misconduct. In case where Government conducts a review and issue an                 <br /><br /><br />
 audit report, Government shall be deemed not to have objected to the                <br /><br /><br />
 Cost Recovery Statement and such Cost Recovery Statement shall be                   <br /><br /><br />
 considered true and correct for Cost Recovery purposes for such calendar            <br /><br /><br />
 year with respect to each item which is not the subject of an exception in          <br /><br /><br />
 such audit report absent material mistake, fraud or willful misconduct.             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
