﻿Section 2 Classification, Definition and Allocation of Costs and Expenditures                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                       All expenditures relating to the Petroleum Operations shall, subject to     <br /><br /><br />
                       Applicable Law be classified, defined and allocated as follows:             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
2.1. Exploration Costs                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
“Exploration Cost" shall consist of all direct and allocated indirect costs                        <br /><br /><br />
incurred in the search for Petroleum in the EPC Area, including but not                            <br /><br /><br />
limited to:                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Aerial, geophysical, geochemical, paleontological, geological,                              <br /><br /><br />
topographical and seismic surveys and studies and their interpretation.                            <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Core hole drilling and water well drilling.                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(c)    Labour, materials and services used in drilling wells with the object of                    <br /><br /><br />
finding new Petroleum Reservoirs or for the purpose of appraising the                              <br /><br /><br />
extent of Petroleum Reservoirs already discovered provided such wells                              <br /><br /><br />
are not completed as producing wells.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(d)    Facilities used solely in support of these purposes including access roads                  <br /><br /><br />
and purchased geological and geophysical information.                                              <br /><br /><br />
(e)    Service Costs allocated to the Exploration Operations as per the                            <br /><br /><br />
provisions of Subsection 2.4 of this Accounting Procedure.                                         <br /><br /><br />
(f)    General and Administrative Expenses allocated to the Exploration                            <br /><br /><br />
Operations as per the provisions of Subsection 2.5 of this Accounting                              <br /><br /><br />
Procedure.                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 2.2. Development and Production Capital Expenditures                                              <br /><br /><br />
 “Development and Production Capital Expenditure” shall consist of all                             <br /><br /><br />
 expenditures incurred in the Development and Production Operations,                               <br /><br /><br />
 including but not limited to:                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    Drilling wells which are completed as producing wells and drilling wells for               <br /><br /><br />
 purposes of producing from a Petroleum Reservoir already discovered                               <br /><br /><br />
 whether these wells are dry or producing.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    Completing wells by way of installation of casing or equipment or                          <br /><br /><br />
 otherwise after a well has been drilled for the purpose of bringing the well                      <br /><br /><br />
 into use as a producing well.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    Intangible drilling costs such as labour, consumable material and services                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 having no salvage value which are incurred in drilling and deepening of                           <br /><br /><br />
 wells for production purposes.                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 (d)    The costs of field facilities such as flow lines, production and treatment                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 units, wellhead equipment, subsurface equipment, enhanced recovery                                <br /><br /><br />
 systems, offshore platforms, Petroleum storage facilities, export terminals                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                          Page 8 of 28                                             <br /><br /><br />
﻿ and piers, harbours and related facilities, and access roads for production        <br /><br /><br />
 activities.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 (e)    Engineering and design studies for field facilities.                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 (f)    Service Costs allocated to the Development and Production Operations        <br /><br /><br />
 as per the provisions of Subsection 2.4 of this Accounting Procedure.              <br /><br /><br />
 (g)    General and Administrative Expenses allocated to the Development and        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 Production Operations as per the provisions of Subsection 2.5 of this              <br /><br /><br />
 Accounting Procedure.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
2.3. Operating Costs                                                                <br /><br /><br />
“Operating Costs" shall consist of all expenditures incurred in the Petroleum       <br /><br /><br />
Operations after the start of the Commercial Production which are other than        <br /><br /><br />
Exploration Costs, Development and Production Capital Expenditures, General         <br /><br /><br />
and Administrative Expenses and Service Costs, including but not limited to:        <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Operating, servicing, maintaining and repairing production and injection     <br /><br /><br />
wells and all field facilities completed during the Development and                 <br /><br /><br />
Production Operations.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Planning, producing, controlling, measuring and testing the flow of          <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum and collecting, gathering, treating, storing and transferring the         <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum from the Petroleum Reservoir to the Delivery Point.                       <br /><br /><br />
(c)    The balance of General and Administrative Expenses and Service Costs         <br /><br /><br />
not allocated to the Exploration Operations or the Development and                  <br /><br /><br />
Production Operations.                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
2.4 Service Costs                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
“Service Costs" shall consist of direct and indirect expenditures in support        <br /><br /><br />
of the Petroleum Operations including warehouses, offices, camps, piers,            <br /><br /><br />
marine vessels, vehicles, motorised rolling equipment, aircraft, fire and           <br /><br /><br />
security stations, workshops, water and sewage plants, power plants,                <br /><br /><br />
housing, community and recreational facilities and furniture, tools and             <br /><br /><br />
equipment used in these activities. Service costs in any calendar year              <br /><br /><br />
shall include the total costs incurred in such year to purchase and/or              <br /><br /><br />
construct said facilities as well as the annual costs to maintain and               <br /><br /><br />
operate the same. All Service costs will be regularly allocated as                  <br /><br /><br />
specified in Subsections 2.1(e), 2.2(f) and 2.3 to Exploration Costs,               <br /><br /><br />
Development and Production Capital Expenditures and Operating Costs.                <br /><br /><br />
Service Costs incurred during the period commencing with the Effective Date and     <br /><br /><br />
ending with the date of approval by MIREM of the first Development Plan for a       <br /><br /><br />
proposed Development and Production Area, shall be fully allocated to               <br /><br /><br />
Exploration Cost. Commencing with the date of approval by MIREM of the first        <br /><br /><br />
Development Plan for a proposed Development and Production Area, and if it          <br /><br /><br />
becomes necessary to allocate Service Costs to or between Petroleum                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
Execution copy                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                      Page 9 of 28                                  <br /><br /><br />
﻿ Operations, such allocation shall be made on an equitable basis in accordance          <br /><br /><br />
 with applicable law, failing agreement, the allocation to be determined by a sole      <br /><br /><br />
 expert in accordance with Article 30 of the EPC.                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
 The Concessionaire shall furnish a description of its allocation procedures            <br /><br /><br />
 pertaining to Service Costs, along with each proposed Development Plan.                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
2.5 General and Administrative Expenses                                                 <br /><br /><br />
“General and Administrative Expenses" shall consist of:                                 <br /><br /><br />
(a)    All main office, field office and general administrative costs in the            <br /><br /><br />
Republic of Mozambique including but not limited to supervisory,                        <br /><br /><br />
accounting and employee relations services.                                             <br /><br /><br />
(b)    An overhead charge for services rendered outside the Republic of                 <br /><br /><br />
Mozambique for managing the Petroleum Operations and for staff advice                   <br /><br /><br />
and assistance including financial, legal, accounting and employee                      <br /><br /><br />
relations services. This charge shall be five percent (5%) of Contract                  <br /><br /><br />
Costs up to five million US dollars (US$5,000,000), three percent (3%) of               <br /><br /><br />
that portion of Contract Costs between five million US dollars                          <br /><br /><br />
(US$5,000,000) and ten million US dollars (US$10,000,000) and one and                   <br /><br /><br />
one half percent (1.5%) of Contract Costs which are in excess of ten                    <br /><br /><br />
million US dollars (US$10,000,000). The contract costs referred to herein               <br /><br /><br />
shall include all Exploration Costs, Development and Production Capital                 <br /><br /><br />
Expenditures, Operating Costs and Service Costs.                                        <br /><br /><br />
(c)    All General and Administrative Expenses will be regularly allocated              <br /><br /><br />
as specified in Subsections 2.1(f), 2.2(g) and 2.3 to Exploration Costs,                <br /><br /><br />
Development and Production Capital Expenditures and Operating Costs.                    <br /><br /><br />
General and Administrative Expenses incurred during the period                          <br /><br /><br />
commencing with the Effective Date and ending with the date of approval                 <br /><br /><br />
by MIREM of the first Development Plan for a proposed Development and                   <br /><br /><br />
Production Area, shall be fully allocated to Exploration Cost.                          <br /><br /><br />
Commencing with the date of approval by MIREM of the first Development                  <br /><br /><br />
Plan for a proposed Development and Production Area, if it becomes                      <br /><br /><br />
necessary to allocate General and Administrative Expenses to or between                 <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations, such allocation shall be made on an equitable                     <br /><br /><br />
basis agreed between the parties in accordance with applicable law,                     <br /><br /><br />
failing agreement, the allocation to be determined by a sole expert in                  <br /><br /><br />
accordance with Article 30 of the EPC.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
The Concessionaire shall furnish a description of its allocation procedures             <br /><br /><br />
pertaining to General and Administrative Expenses, along with each                      <br /><br /><br />
proposed Development Plan                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
2.6 Decommissioning Fund                                                                <br /><br /><br />
For the purpose of costs related to the implementation of a Decommissioning Plan a      <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Fund shall be established for each Development and Production           <br /><br /><br />
Area, commencing from the calendar quarter in whichever of the following situations     <br /><br /><br />
first occur:                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
Execution copy                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                         Page 10 of 28                                  <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                  a)    the Petroleum Produced has reached 50% of the aggregate                     <br /><br /><br />
                                  recoverable resources as determined in an approved Development                    <br /><br /><br />
                                  Plan and any successive reappraisal of such initial recoverable                   <br /><br /><br />
                                  reserves; or                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                  b)    five (5) years prior to the expiry or surrender of this EPC or the use of   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                  any facility for the purpose of extracting Petroleum from a Production            <br /><br /><br />
                                  and Development Area within this EPC is permanently terminated.                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 For every subsequent calendar quarter in which Petroleum is produced, the                                          <br /><br /><br />
 Concessionaire shall charge as Operating Costs a portion of the estimated future                                   <br /><br /><br />
 cost of decommissioning.                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 The amount to be deposited in the Decommissioning Fund for a calendar quarter                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 shall be charged as Operating Costs subject to the Cost Recovery limitation                                        <br /><br /><br />
 stipulated in article 9.5 of the EPC and calculated in the following manner:                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 QD = (ECA X (EPR/CPP)) - DFB                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 where:                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 QD is the amount of funds to be transferred to                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 the Decommissioning Fund in respect of the                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 relevant calendar quarter;                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 ECA is the estimated cost of abandonment                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 operations established pursuant to the                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
 Decommissioning Plan;                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 EPR is the estimated remaining Petroleum                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 reserves to be recovered from the end of                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 the calendar quarter in which the                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 Decommissioning Fund was opened;                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 CPP is the cumulative production of Petroleum                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
 from the end of the calendar quarter in                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
 which the Decommissioning Fund was                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 opened;                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
 DFB is the Decommissioning Fund balance at                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 the end of the previous calendar quarter.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />

﻿Section 3 Costs, Expenses, Expenditures and Credits of the Concessionaire                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
3.1 Subject to Applicable Law, costs recoverable without further approval of                                       <br /><br /><br />
the Government.                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                 Subject to the provisions of the EPC and applicable law, the                                      <br /><br /><br />
                 Concessionaire shall bear and pay the following costs and expenses in                             <br /><br /><br />
                 respect of the Petroleum Operations. These costs and expenses will be                             <br /><br /><br />
                 classified under the headings referred to in Section 2. They are                                  <br /><br /><br />
                 recoverable by the Concessionaire under the EPC.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                 (a) Surface Rights                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                 This covers all direct costs attributable to the acquisition, renewal or                          <br /><br /><br />
                 relinquishment of surface rights acquired and maintained in force for the                         <br /><br /><br />
                 EPC Area.                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                 (b)    Labour and Associated Labour Costs                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                 (i)    gross salaries and wages including bonuses and premiums of the                             <br /><br /><br />
                 Concessionaire's employees directly engaged in the Petroleum                                      <br /><br /><br />
                 Operations, irrespective of the location of such employees, it being                              <br /><br /><br />
                 understood that in the case of those personnel only a portion of                                  <br /><br /><br />
                 whose time is dedicated to the Petroleum Operations, only that                                    <br /><br /><br />
                 pro-rata portion of applicable salaries, wages and fringe benefits                                <br /><br /><br />
                 will be charged;                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                 (ii)    the Concessionaire’s costs regarding holiday, vacation, sickness                          <br /><br /><br />
                 and disability payments applicable to the salaries and wages                                      <br /><br /><br />
                 chargeable under (i) above.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                 (iii)    expenses or contributions made pursuant to assessments or                                <br /><br /><br />
                 obligations imposed under the laws of the Republic of                                             <br /><br /><br />
                 Mozambique which are applicable to the Concessionaire's cost of                                   <br /><br /><br />
                 salaries and wages chargeable under (i) above;                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                 (iv)    the Concessionaire's cost of established plans for employees' life                        <br /><br /><br />
                 insurance, hospitalisation, pensions, and other benefits of a like                                <br /><br /><br />
                 nature customarily granted to the Concessionaire's employees;                                     <br /><br /><br />
                 (v)    reasonable travel and personal expenses of employees of the                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                 Concessionaire including those made for travel and relocation of                                  <br /><br /><br />
                 the expatriate employees and their families assigned to the                                       <br /><br /><br />
                 Republic of Mozambique, all of which shall be in accordance with                                  <br /><br /><br />
                 the Concessionaire's normal practice;                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                 (vi)    any personal income taxes of the Republic of Mozambique                                   <br /><br /><br />
                 incurred by employees and paid or reimbursed by the                                               <br /><br /><br />
                 Concessionaire.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                 (c)    Transportation                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                            The cost of transportation of employees, equipment, materials and      <br /><br /><br />
                                            supplies necessary for the conduct of the Petroleum Operations.        <br /><br /><br />

                         proportion of the general material, management, technical and          <br /><br /><br />
                         other costs of the Affiliated Company, and the amount which is the     <br /><br /><br />
                         direct cost of providing the services concerned. If necessary,         <br /><br /><br />
                         certified evidence regarding the basis of prices charged may be        <br /><br /><br />
                         obtained from the auditors of the Affiliated Company.                  <br /><br /><br />

        (e)              Material                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                         (i)    General                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                         So far as is practicable and consistent with efficient, economical     <br /><br /><br />
                         and internationally accepted operational requirements, only such       <br /><br /><br />
                         material shall be purchased or furnished by the Concessionaire for     <br /><br /><br />
                         use in the Petroleum Operations as may be required for use in the      <br /><br /><br />
                         reasonably foreseeable future and to the extent that such              <br /><br /><br />
                         purchase or supply are in accordance with the EPC.                     <br /><br /><br />
                         (ii)    Warranty of Material                                           <br /><br /><br />

7.1                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
The Concessionaire shall prepare with respect to each calendar quarter a                                                          <br /><br /><br />

Subsection 7.1(b)).                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(d)    Quantity and value of Cost Petroleum taken proportionally in Crude oil                                                     <br /><br /><br />
and Natural Gas and disposed of by the Concessionaire for the quarter in                                                          <br /><br /><br />
question.                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
(e)    EPC costs recovered for the quarter in question.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(f)    Total cumulative amount of EPC costs recovered up to the end of the                                                        <br /><br /><br />
quarter in question.                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(g)    Amount of recoverable EPC costs to be carried forward into the next                                                        <br /><br /><br />
quarter.                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                               The Cost Recovery Statement of each quarter shall be submitted to the              <br /><br /><br />
                                               Government no later than thirty (30) days after the end of such quarter.           <br /><br /><br />

﻿Section 8 Statement of Expenditure and Receipts                                                                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
8.1                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
The Concessionaire shall prepare with respect to each calendar quarter a                                       <br /><br /><br />
statement of expenditures and receipts under the EPC (hereinafter                                              <br /><br /><br />
referred to as the “Statement of Expenditure and Receipts”). The                                               <br /><br /><br />
statement will distinguish between Exploration Costs, Development and                                          <br /><br /><br />
Production Capital Expenditures, Operating Costs, decommissioning                                              <br /><br /><br />
costs and the balance of the Decommissioning Fund and will identify                                            <br /><br /><br />
major items of expenditures within these categories. The statement will                                        <br /><br /><br />
show the following:                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Actual expenditures and receipts for the quarter in question.                                           <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Cumulative expenditure and receipts for the budget year in question.                                    <br /><br /><br />
(c)    Latest forecast cumulative expenditures at the year end.                                                <br /><br /><br />
(d)    Variations between budget forecast and latest forecast and explanations                                 <br /><br /><br />
thereof.                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                   The Statement of Expenditure and Receipts of each calendar quarter shall    <br /><br /><br />
                                   be submitted to the Government no later than thirty (30) days after the     <br /><br /><br />
                                   end of such quarter.                                                        <br /><br /><br />

﻿Section 10 Budget Statement                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
10.1                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                  The Concessionaire shall prepare an annual budget statement                                             <br /><br /><br />
                  (hereinafter referred to as the “Budget Statement”). This will distinguish                              <br /><br /><br />
                  between Exploration Costs, Development and Production Capital                                           <br /><br /><br />
                  Expenditures and Operating Costs and will show the following:                                           <br /><br /><br />
                  (a)    Forecast expenditures and receipts for the budget year under the EPC.                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                  (b)    Forecast cumulative expenditures and receipts to the end of the said                             <br /><br /><br />
                  budget year.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                  (c)    A schedule showing the most important individual items of forecast                               <br /><br /><br />
                  Development and Production Capital Expenditures for the said budget                                     <br /><br /><br />
                  year.                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

                                           to each budget year no less than ninety (90) days before the start of the      <br /><br /><br />
                                           year except in the case of the first year of the EPC when the Budget           <br /><br /><br />
                                           Statement shall be submitted within thirty (30) days of the Effective Date.    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
10.3                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />

                                           details of the Budget Statement may require changes in the light of            <br /><br /><br />
                                           existing circumstances and nothing herein contained shall limit the            <br /><br /><br />
                                           flexibility to make such changes. Consistent with the foregoing the            <br /><br /><br />
                                           revision of said Statement is provided for annually.                           <br /><br /><br />

﻿Section 11 Long Range Plan and Forecast                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
The Concessionaire shall prepare and submit for information and planning            <br /><br /><br />
purpose to the Government either one or both of the following two (2) long          <br /><br /><br />
range plans, whichever is appropriate:                                              <br /><br /><br />
11.1    Exploration Plan                                                            <br /><br /><br />
During the Exploration Period, the Concessionaire shall prepare an                  <br /><br /><br />
Exploration Plan for each period of three (3) calendar years commencing             <br /><br /><br />
as of the first day of January following the Effective Date (hereinafter            <br /><br /><br />
referred to as the "Exploration Plan”) which shall contain the following            <br /><br /><br />
information:                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Estimated Exploration Costs showing outlays for each of the three (3)        <br /><br /><br />
calendar years covered by the Exploration Plan.                                     <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Details of seismic operations planned for each such year.                    <br /><br /><br />
(c)    Details of all drilling activities planned for each such year.               <br /><br /><br />
(d)    Details of infrastructure utilisation and requirements.                      <br /><br /><br />
The first such Exploration Plan shall also include the above information for        <br /><br /><br />
the period starting on the Effective Date and ending on the last day of             <br /><br /><br />
December of that calendar year.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
The Exploration Plan shall be revised at the beginning of each calendar             <br /><br /><br />
year following of the Effective Date. The Concessionaire shall prepare              <br /><br /><br />
and submit to the Government the first Exploration Plan within sixty (60)           <br /><br /><br />
days of the Effective Date and thereafter shall prepare and submit to the           <br /><br /><br />
Government no less than forty-five (45) days before the end of each                 <br /><br /><br />
calendar year following the Effective Date a revised Exploration Plan.              <br /><br /><br />
11.2    Development Forecast                                                        <br /><br /><br />
The Concessionaire shall prepare a development forecast for each period             <br /><br /><br />
of five (5) calendar years (hereinafter referred to as the “Development             <br /><br /><br />
Forecast”) commencing as of the first day of January following the date             <br /><br /><br />
when the first development plan is approved and the Concessionaire                  <br /><br /><br />
commences the implementation of such plan.                                          <br /><br /><br />
The Development Forecast shall contain the following information:                   <br /><br /><br />
(a)    Forecast of Development and Production Capital Expenditures for each of      <br /><br /><br />
the five (5) calendar years.                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(b)    Forecast of Operating Costs for each such calendar year.                     <br /><br /><br />
(c)    Forecast of Petroleum production for each such calendar year.                <br /><br /><br />
(d)    Forecast of number and types of personnel employed in the Petroleum          <br /><br /><br />
Operations in the Republic of Mozambique.                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 I' xcciifioii                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                       Page 25 of 28                <br /><br /><br />
﻿(e)    Description of proposed Petroleum marketing arrangements.                <br /><br /><br />
(f)    Description of main technologies employed.                               <br /><br /><br />
(g)    Description of working relationship of the Concessionaire to the         <br /><br /><br />
Government.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
The Development Forecast shall be revised at the beginning of each              <br /><br /><br />
calendar year commencing as of the second year of the first Development         <br /><br /><br />
Forecast. The Concessionaire shall prepare and submit to the                    <br /><br /><br />
Government the first Development Forecast within one hundred and                <br /><br /><br />
twenty (120) days from the date when the first development plan is              <br /><br /><br />
approved or deemed to have been approved by the Management                      <br /><br /><br />
Committee and the Concessionaire commences the implementation of                <br /><br /><br />
such plan and thereafter shall prepare and submit a revised Development         <br /><br /><br />
Forecast to the Government no later than forty-five (45) days before each       <br /><br /><br />
calendar year commencing as of the second year of the first Development         <br /><br /><br />
Forecast.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
11.3 Changes of Plan and Forecast                                               <br /><br /><br />
It is recognised by the Concessionaire and the Government that the              <br /><br /><br />
details of the Exploration Plan and Development Forecast may require            <br /><br /><br />
changes in the light of existing circumstances and nothing herein               <br /><br /><br />
contained shall limit the flexibility to make such changes. Consistent with     <br /><br /><br />
the foregoing the revision of said Plan and Forecast is provided for            <br /><br /><br />
annually.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />

                                                         Bank Guarantee                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
[Date]                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
Ministry of Mineral Resources                                                                <br /><br /><br />
The Minister of Mineral Resources                                                            <br /><br /><br />
Av. Fernao de Magalhaes, 34, 1                                                               <br /><br /><br />
Maputo, Mozambique                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
1.    We understand that on_2006, the Government of the Republic of                          <br /><br /><br />
Mozambique, Empresa Nacional de Hidrocarbonetos, (ENH) E.P and Eni East                      <br /><br /><br />
Africa S.p.A. (the latter also the “Guaranteed Party”) entered into an Exploration and       <br /><br /><br />
Production Concession Contract for Area 4 of the Rovuma Basin offshore of                    <br /><br /><br />
Mozambique (the “EPC”). For purposes of this Bank Guarantee, ENH and the                     <br /><br /><br />
Guaranteed Party are collectively referred to as the “Concessionaire”. Capitalised           <br /><br /><br />
words not defined in this Bank Guarantee shall have the meaning ascribed to them             <br /><br /><br />
in the EPC.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
2.    We, the undersigned [BANK LEGAL NAME] (the “Bank"), hereby, save for the               <br /><br /><br />
conditions stipulated below in clause 5, unconditionally and irrevocably guarantee in        <br /><br /><br />
favour of the Government of the Republic of Mozambique (the “Government") the due            <br /><br /><br />
and punctual payment of all sums owed to the Government and unpaid by the                    <br /><br /><br />

work commitment in relation to the...............Exploration Period, up to a maximum         <br /><br /><br />
of United States_(US$ _,000,000).                                                            <br /><br /><br />

time upon delivery to the Bank of a certificate from the Guaranteed Party                    <br /><br /><br />
countersigned on behalf of the Government setting forth the amount of such                   <br /><br /><br />

                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
correct the conditions of non-compliance and has failed to do so.                                  <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                ANNEX “E”                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                        Parent Company Guarantee                                               <br /><br /><br />
THIS GUARANTEE is made the day of 20[ ]                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
BY and BETWEEN                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(1)    Eni S.p.A, a limited liability company established under the laws of Italy (the                         <br /><br /><br />
"Guarantor"), in favour of                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(2)    THE GOVERNMENT OF THE REPUBLIC OF MOZAMBIQUE, herein represented                                        <br /><br /><br />
by the Minister for Mineral Resources and Energy (the "Government");                                           <br /><br /><br />
(each a "Party" and collectively the "Parties")                                                                <br /><br /><br />
WHEREAS                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
A On_, the Government, Empresa Nacional de Hidrocarbonetos, (ENH)                                              <br /><br /><br />
EP and Eni East Africa S.p.A. (the “Concessionaire") entered into an Exploration                               <br /><br /><br />
and Production Concession Contract (the "EPC") for Area 4 of the Rovuma Basin,                                 <br /><br /><br />
offshore of Mozambique.                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
B The Guarantor is the ultimate parent company of Eni East Africa S.p.A. (the                                  <br /><br /><br />
“Company”).                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
C The Government requires that the due and proper performance of the Company                                   <br /><br /><br />
Obligations shall be guaranteed by the Guarantor under the terms of this Guarantee                             <br /><br /><br />
and the Guarantor is willing to grant this Guarantee.                                                          <br /><br /><br />
NOW IT IS HEREBY AGREED AS FOLLOWS:                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
1 DEFINITIONS AND INTERPRETATION                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                      1.1    "Company Obligations" means any obligations limited to the Company’s              <br /><br /><br />
                      Participating Interest in the EPC and related to or arising out of the Company’          <br /><br /><br />
                      activities relevant to Petroleum Operations during any period occurring any time         <br /><br /><br />
                      after completion of the Exploration Period up to and including final                     <br /><br /><br />
                      implementation of decommissioning of facilities.                                         <br /><br /><br />
                      1.2    “Third Party Claimant” means a natural person who is a citizen of the Republic    <br /><br /><br />
                      of Mozambique or any legal entity established and registered pursuant to                 <br /><br /><br />
                      Mozambican law, with its headquarters in Mozambique and having at least 50%              <br /><br /><br />
                      of its share capital held by citizens of Republic of Mozambique.                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 Terms defined in the EPC shall have the same meaning when used in this Guarantee.                             <br /><br /><br />
 Words referred to in the singular shall include the plural and vice versa.                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                          /                    <br /><br /><br />
﻿2 GUARANTEE                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
       2.1    The Guarantor irrevocably and unconditionally guarantees, subject to all the                          <br /><br /><br />
       other terms of this Guarantee, that if the Company fails, in whole or in part, to                            <br /><br /><br />
       perform any of the Company Obligations towards the Government, and to                                        <br /><br /><br />
       satisfy any claim of a Third Party Claimant made against the Company as a                                    <br /><br /><br />
       result or consequence of the Company’s acts or omissions in carrying out the                                 <br /><br /><br />
       Company Obligations (each of the Government, and Third Party Claimant                                        <br /><br /><br />
       being hereinafter collectively referred to as the “Beneficiaries”), the Guarantor                            <br /><br /><br />
       shall as soon as reasonably practicable following a demand made in                                           <br /><br /><br />
       accordance with clause 3, take such steps itself as shall be necessary:                                      <br /><br /><br />
       (a)    to perform such Company Obligation or remedy such breach; or                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
       (b)    where such failure or breach is not capable of remedy, restore performance of                         <br /><br /><br />
       the breached Company Obligation.                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
       2.2    This Guarantee shall become effective thirty (30) days after the approval of                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
       the Development Plan and shall terminate on termination of all relevant                                      <br /><br /><br />
       Petroleum Operations subject to the applicable law and the EPC.                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
       2.3    Upon termination of this Guarantee the Guarantor shall have no further                                <br /><br /><br />
       liability whatsoever to the Beneficiaries under or in connection with this                                   <br /><br /><br />
       Guarantee save in respect of any breach notified by the Beneficiaries in                                     <br /><br /><br />
       accordance with clause 3 this Guarantee prior to its termination.                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 3 DEMANDS                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                          3.1    The Beneficiaries shall notify the Guarantor in writing when a breach of a         <br /><br /><br />
                          Company Obligation has occurred and such notice shall contain a description               <br /><br /><br />
                          of such breach.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                          3.2    Subject to clauses 4 and 7 of this Guarantee, if the Company fails to remedy a     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                          breach specified in a notice given under clause 3.1 within fourteen (14) days             <br /><br /><br />
                          of receipt of such notice by the Guarantor, the Beneficiaries may then make a             <br /><br /><br />
                          demand in writing to the Guarantor that shall (i) set out the alleged breach of           <br /><br /><br />
                          the Company Obligation(s); and (ii) require the Guarantor to take such steps              <br /><br /><br />
                          as are provided in clause 2 of this Guarantee.                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 4 RIGHTS AND OBLIGATIONS                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
 4.1    The Beneficiaries shall be obliged before exercising any of the rights, powers or                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 remedies conferred upon it in respect of the Guarantor by this Guarantee or by                                     <br /><br /><br />
 law:                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 4.1.1    to notify the Company of the breach of a Company Obligation;                                              <br /><br /><br />
 4.1.2    if the Company:                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                 2                                  <br /><br /><br />
﻿(a)    in the case of a claim by the Government, disputes the breach notified by the                                               <br /><br /><br />
Government, to have obtained an arbitral award or expert determination                                                             <br /><br /><br />
confirming such breach by the Company; or                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
(b)    in the case of a claim by a Third Party Claimant, disputes the breach notified                                              <br /><br /><br />
by such Third Party Claimant, to have obtained a court judgment or order,                                                          <br /><br /><br />
provided that such judgment or order of a court has been issued against the                                                        <br /><br /><br />
Company and such judgment or order is final and non-appealable; and                                                                <br /><br /><br />
4.1.3 to make or file any claim or proof in winding-up or dissolution of the Company (to                                           <br /><br /><br />
the extent applicable).                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
5 LIMITATIONS                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
5.1 The obligations of the Guarantor under this Guarantee shall not be discharged                                                  <br /><br /><br />
or impaired by any act or omission or any other event or circumstances                                                             <br /><br /><br />
whatsoever (whether or not known to the Company, the Guarantor or the                                                              <br /><br /><br />
Beneficiaries) which would or might (but for this clause 5) operate to impair or                                                   <br /><br /><br />
discharge the Guarantor's liability under this Guarantee, including, but without                                                   <br /><br /><br />
limitation:                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
5.1.1    any of the Company Obligations being or becoming illegal or invalid, in                                                   <br /><br /><br />
any respect;                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
5.1.2    any granting of time (or other indulgence) to the Company or any other                                                    <br /><br /><br />
person; or                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
5.1.3    any amendment to or variation, waiver or release of, any of the terms of the                                              <br /><br /><br />
EPC to the extent that such amendment, variation, waiver or release is                                                             <br /><br /><br />
made with the Guarantor's prior written consent.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 6 ASSIGNMENT AND SUCCESSORS                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 6.1    Any benefit of this Guarantee shall not be assignable by the Beneficiaries to                                              <br /><br /><br />
 any person.                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 6.2    The Guarantor may not assign its rights and obligations under this Guarantee                                               <br /><br /><br />
 without the prior written consent of the Government.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
 7 LIMITATION AND MAXIMUM LIABILITY OF GUARANTOR                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                    7.1                        Notwithstanding any other provisions of this Guarantee, the Guarantor shall         <br /><br /><br />
                                               have all of the rights, limitations, defences including, without limitation, all    <br /><br /><br />
                                               rights of set off, available to the Company under the EPC or at law in the case     <br /><br /><br />
                                               of a claim by a Third Party Claimant in relation to any demand made under           <br /><br /><br />
                                               clause 3.2 of this Guarantee In no circumstances shall the Guarantor be liable      <br /><br /><br />
                                               to pay any amount under this Guarantee which is greater than the Company            <br /><br /><br />
                                               would have been liable to pay if the Company had performed the Company              <br /><br /><br />
                                               Obligations.                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                           3                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
﻿ 7.2 Notwithstanding any other provision of this Guarantee, the Beneficiaries prior         <br /><br /><br />
 to making any demand or any attempt to collect under this Guarantee, shall                 <br /><br /><br />
 first pursue collection from the Company and shall exhaust all resources                   <br /><br /><br />
 against and liquidation of the Company assets, including but not limited to any            <br /><br /><br />
 applicable insurance coverage available to satisfy any Company Obligations.                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
8 GOVERNING LAW AND JURISDICTION                                                            <br /><br /><br />
This Guarantee shall be governed by and construed in accordance with the laws               <br /><br /><br />
of the Republic of Mozambique. The provisions of Article 30 of the EPC shall                <br /><br /><br />
apply 'mutatis mutandis' to this Guarantee in respect of all disputes between the           <br /><br /><br />
Government, the Guarantor or the Company.                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
